Song Ziwen's Remarks After Arriving in Hankou 50

Hankou Correspondence: Finance Minister Song Ziwen arrived in Hankou at 3 PM today, after traveling by air from Shanghai on a postal flight that departed at 7 AM. He was accompanied by Qian Dajun, Commander of the 3rd Training Division, and Li Jihong, former Director of the Hubei Finance Department. It is reported that Song's visit to Hankou was not telegraphed in advance, so the important figures of Wuhan were unaware of it. Chen Shao嬀, Finance Special Commissioner, had even taken a steamer to Beijing the day before to meet Song, and so they missed each other. After Song arrived in Hankou, he was received by Li Muqing, Chief of the Special Tax Office, and stayed at the Provincial Bank Building. That evening, he went to the Executive Headquarters to meet with Director He Yingqin, where they spoke for about two hours before he returned to his residence. I assumed that Song's visit must be for an important mission, so I went to visit him and was received by Song, who spoke as follows: "Since my last visit to Hankou, nearly a year has passed. Although I have received telegram reports about the recent financial situation in Hubei Province, I am not fully aware of it. Therefore, after inspecting Zhenjiang, Hangzhou, and Shanghai, I took the opportunity to come to Hankou to examine the latest situation for reference. This is one of the reasons for my visit to Hankou. Secondly, the Ping-Han Railway war is making rapid progress, and the joint suppression of bandits in the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi has also begun. The issue of military pay is extremely important, and it is urgent to come to Hankou to discuss everything with Director He of the Executive Headquarters. Thirdly, there are the salt tax loans and the promotion of short-term treasury bonds. The use of salt tax loans is for the suppression of bandits in the three provinces, and the issuance of short-term treasury bonds is a preparation for all facilities after the military is settled. Both are important. This time, I will discuss the methods of promoting treasury bonds with the local authorities here, and I will also consult with the banking community to ensure that the salt tax loans can proceed without hindrance." (August 22nd)

Martial Law in Wuhan to be Lifted 51

Hankou Correspondence: Wuhan has been under martial law since it was declared on the 30th of last month, for more than twenty days. In the meantime, martial law decrees have been promulgated, emergency inspections have been carried out, and secret Communist Party organs have been closed down, and important Communist Party members have been executed. The bustling market has suddenly taken on a solemn appearance. The Wuhan Garrison Command, with a large army gathered and defenses consolidated, originally intended to lift martial law immediately, but because rumors were still rampant and people's hearts were uneasy, the period of martial law was moderately extended to ensure preparedness. Recently, most of the Communists have been arrested and are being sentenced separately. The date of the uprising (August 14th) has also passed peacefully. The rumors in the city have completely subsided, and the Garrison Command has decided to lift martial law in the shortest possible time, restoring the previous state of covert alert. As for the captured bandits and communists, more than sixty people have been shot or beheaded successively. There are still many in prison. Today, Wang Duqing and other eighteen people who were confirmed to be important Communist Party members and the bandit Huang Benqing were executed by shooting, and their crimes were announced as follows: (1) According to the Hubei Higher Court, the 25 Communist Party members including Wang Duqing and Guo Yukang were transferred to the Garrison Command along with the case files, requesting that they be handled in accordance with the secret orders of the National Government. After a detailed review of the original cases, it was determined that Wang Duqing and other eighteen people had indeed joined the Communist Party and were responsible for their work. Wang Duqing served as the commander of the six counties in southern Hubei, presiding over the uprising. Guo Yukang, Chen Xiyan, and Zou Jiyu led the masses in the uprising, destroying railways, attacking cities, and killing people. Zhang Renyu, Lei Zhen, Ku Jihua, Wu Peifu, Rao Minggan, Cheng Xielin, Meng Sheng, Gao Zhang Yingtang, and Zhou Yeshi colluded in the uprising, cruelly killing innocent people. Liang Muxin conspired to kill, set fire, and rob. Liu Jiusong colluded with bandits and looted at will. Liu Antang colluded with others to carry guns and destroy the dyke administration. Huang Jiuzhi gathered bandits to organize an uprising. Zeng Puchen moved the regiment guns and secretly plotted wrongdoing. All the evidence is conclusive and unforgivable by law. According to the court, Wang Duqing collaborated with He Kong in prison, claiming to be the leader of the Communist Party. Zeng Puchen served as secretary in prison, and the others, such as Guo Yukang, either served as commanders or engaged in propaganda and collusion, repeatedly launching uprisings. The circumstances were particularly serious and unavoidable under the law. In accordance with the National Government's Secret Order No. 1, they were all sentenced to death to uphold the law and deter others. In addition to signing the order to bring the criminals to the execution ground to verify their identities and execute them by shooting, this is hereby announced for general knowledge. (2) According to the report from the Inspection Department of the Garrison Command, the bandit Huang Benqing was brought to the Garrison Command. According to Huang Benqing's confession, he admitted to kidnapping people for ransom and looting with his gang in the Daijia Township area of Mianyang. His crimes were heinous and he should be sentenced to death in accordance with Article 2 of the Provisional Regulations for the Punishment of Bandits to serve as a warning. In addition to supervising the extraction of Huang Benqing to verify his identity and tie him to the execution ground for execution by shooting, this is hereby announced for general knowledge. (August 22nd)

Wuhan Municipal Government Established 52

Mayor Xiong Bingkun Scheduled to Take Office

Hankou Correspondence: The Wuhan Municipal Government, after being resolved to be established by the Provincial Government and with the appointment of Committee Member Xiong Bingkun as Mayor, has finally been completed after a long period of preparation. It officially began operations on the 20th. The original organization of the government was to establish a Secretariat, a Finance Bureau, a Public Works Bureau, a Social Affairs Section, a Health Section, and a branch accounting office and a city treasury. Now it has been slightly changed. In addition to retaining the Finance and Public Works Bureaus, the Secretariat has added a General Affairs Section and a Documentation Section, and the Social Affairs and Health Sections have also been changed to sections. The branch accounting office and the city treasury will not be established for the time being, and a Finance Section will be established to manage them. In addition, a Counsellor's Office has been added. The directors of the bureaus have not yet been appointed, only the Secretary-Director Xia Fuchu, Assistant Secretary Wang Sichang, Counsellors Lu Yu and Huang Jiqing, General Affairs Section Chief Tan Changzhao, Documentation Section Chief Liu Yuancong, Finance Section Chief Hu Zhendong, Social Affairs Section Chief Jiang Bingzhong, and Health Section Chief Zhu Baoguang have reported to the government for work on the 20th. When the government was established, I visited an important official and asked which bureau would be established first and when the mayor would take office. According to the conversation, the Finance Bureau will be established first. The establishment of the Public Works Bureau is important, but it may have to be postponed due to financial difficulties. The date of the mayor's inauguration has not yet been determined, but it is planned for the first of next month. A request has been submitted to the Provincial Government and the Executive Yuan to send officials to administer the oath. If they are appointed within the next few days, the swearing-in ceremony can be held on the first of next month, otherwise it cannot be scheduled. (August 20th)

Joint Bandit Suppression Plan for Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi 53

Hankou Correspondence: After the recovery of Changsha, the authorities felt that the bandit communists were rampant and were eager to suppress them. Therefore, there was a joint bandit suppression plan for the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi, which was actively prepared by Director He Yingqin of the Executive Headquarters, with the aim of completely eliminating them in the shortest possible time. The plan has now been drafted and will be ordered to the troops of the three provinces for strict implementation. The recent bandit suppression situation, the general outline of the plan, and the strength of the bandit army are explored and recorded separately below.

Strength of the Bandit Army: The most prominent Communist bandits entrenched in the border areas of the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi are He Long, Peng Dehuai, Zhu De, Mao Zedong, etc. The next are Huang Gonglue, Wu Zhonghao, Chen Yi, Lin Biao, Fang Zhimin, Duan Qifeng, Peng Qingquan, Shao Shiping, Li Wenbiao, and Duan Yuequan, etc. Although they have very few guns, the rabble amounts to more than 30,000 people. The exact number of other scattered bandits is still unknown. This time, Peng Dehuai's forces captured Changsha, and Zhu De, Mao Zedong, etc. also launched an uprising in Jiangxi. The Communist bandits between Hankou and Jiujiang were even thinking of taking the opportunity to launch an uprising. Later, when the Peng bandits withdrew from Changsha and fled to Pingliu, and Zhu Mao's plan to seize Nanchang also failed, the bandit forces were slightly suppressed. Now the Peng bandits have fled to Jiangxi, although they have not yet established contact with Zhu Mao, they are not far apart. Judging from the situation, they will definitely try to unite and resist the government troops. However, their strength has been greatly reduced, and many of those who were coerced into joining have also fled. Surrounded by government troops on all sides, it is difficult to think that they can succeed again.

Bandit Suppression Arrangement: This time, the troops of Hunan Province to suppress the Peng bandits include the divisions of Liu Jianxu, Luo Fanyi, Wei Su Zhong, and Tao Guang, and the brigades of Chen Guangzhong, etc. The troops of Hubei Province include the divisions of Gong Bingfan and Luo Lin, and a part of Peng Qibiao's brigade. Jiangxi Province has also dispatched the division of Zhang Huizan and the brigade of Dai Yue to intercept and encircle them in different directions. The encirclement has already been formed. Currently, the divisions of Luo Lin and Gong Bingfan are distributed along the Yuezhou-Miluo-Pingjiang line, and the divisions of Liu Jianxu and Luo Fanying are distributed along the Liuyang-Liling line. According to aerial reconnaissance reports, the bandit suppression troops have established contact with each other, forming an arc of hundreds of miles from Xiushui and Tonggu in Jiangxi to Pingjiang, Liuyang, and Liling in Hunan. The bandits in Wanzai and other places are already heavily surrounded. The scattered bandits in other places are also in a state of utter disarray. After the aircraft dropped bombs along the way, many were killed.

Executive Headquarters Meeting: The Wuhan Executive Headquarters convened a temporary meeting on the evening of the 16th to discuss the bandit suppression measures for Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi. The attendees included He Guoguang, Chief of Staff of the Executive Headquarters, Wang Lun, Deputy Chief of Staff, the chiefs of various departments, and various counselors. Director He Yingqin was inspecting the fortress at Shekou and was replaced by He Guoguang as chairman. The result of the discussion was that He Yingqin will convene a bandit suppression conference for the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi in the near future, bringing together the military and political leaders of the three provinces to jointly discuss the implementation measures. If Lu Dipin, Chairman of the Jiangxi Provincial Government, and He Jian, Chairman of the Hunan Provincial Government, are unable to attend the meeting due to their involvement in bandit suppression, they will send their responsible representatives to attend. As for the special bandit suppression agency, it was originally planned to establish a Bandit Suppression Office for the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi attached to the Executive Headquarters, but to save expenses, a Pacification Section will be temporarily added to the Executive Headquarters. Zhou Shaojin, a senior staff officer of the Ministry of Military Affairs, has been appointed to temporarily preside over it.

Pacification Plan: He Yingqin has completed the draft of the pacification plan for the three provinces and submitted it to the Commander-in-Chief for review and implementation. The general allocation of military strength is to request Commander-in-Chief Chiang to transfer three divisions to garrison Wuhan, to be deployed at any time. The remaining Xie Bin, Peng Qibiao, Li Yunlong, Guo Rudong, Liu Xiang, Lai Xinhui, Dai Minquan, Xu Dezhao, and Fan Shisheng stationed in Hubei, and Luo Lin, Gong Bingfan, Wei Su Zhong, Tao Guang, Luo Fanying, Liu Jianxu, Chen Guangzhong, and Dai Douyuan stationed in Hunan, and Zhang Huizan, Dai Yue, and Deng Ying and other divisions and brigades stationed in Jiangxi, will all be responsible for pacification, totaling no less than eighteen divisions. As for the order of suppression, it is planned to divide it into three periods: the first period is to suppress the Communist bandits in Hunan, the second period is to suppress the Communist bandits in Jiangxi, and the third period is to suppress the Communist bandits in Hubei. It is expected that it will be completed within two months. Representatives Coming and Going: After He Yingqin finalized the pacification plan for the three provinces, in addition to telegraphing the main points to Commander-in-Chief Jiang, he also handed over the detailed plan to Hu Yimin, the representative of the Seventh Army, to present to Commander-in-Chief Jiang at the front. Hu has already flown to the front on the 17th. He Jian, Chairman of the Hunan Provincial Government, also sent representative Yu Xiangsan to Hankou to meet He and ask for instructions. He returned to Hunan on the 18th with the plan to report to He Jian. Xie Muhan, representative of Jiangxi Province, also came to Hankou at the same time and returned to Jiangxi on the 17th to report. On the 18th, Director He sent Jia Botao, a counselor of the Executive Headquarters, to Nanchang to take charge of liaison for the Ninth Route Army, and sent Leng Xin to Beijing to report everything to the Executive Yuan of the National Government. Jia and Leng left for the east together on the evening of the 18th. (August 19th)

Nanchang Correspondence: The three-province joint suppression of Peng Dehuai, Zhu De, and Mao Zedong began after Director He issued the general offensive order on the 16th. The Wei and Liu units of the Fourth Route Army and Luo Lin's division advanced in three directions from Pingliu to Xiushui, Tonggu, and Wanzai. The 18th Division of the Ninth Route Army, in addition to having the 54th Brigade firmly guard the Jiangxi border, Dai Yue's unit had already arrived in Xiutong, engaging in interception. It is reported that Commander-in-Chief Lu recently received a telegram from Yang Mianzhong, Secretary-General of the Provincial Government, from Beijing, stating that President Tan had recently telegraphed Commander-in-Chief Jiang requesting the addition of elite troops to Jiangxi to assist in the suppression. Commander-in-Chief Jiang had previously agreed to draw the 1st Training Division to Jiangxi and it will be able to set off in the near future. After the arrival of the division, the bandit suppression can be carried out on a large scale. In order to ensure that the bandit suppression troops of the three provinces are connected as one, Director He, in addition to telegraphing Hunan and Jiangxi to send personnel to the Wuhan Executive Headquarters to form a Pacification Section, also convened a bandit suppression conference for the three provinces. The Jiangxi Provincial Party Headquarters has appointed Yin Jingrang to participate, and the Ninth Route Army has appointed staff officer Yang Duo to participate. As for the situation of the Communist bandits, it is reported that most of Zhu Mao's forces are still in Wanzai, and they still have plans to unite with the Peng bandits and flee to Hunan. A group of Communist bandits in the Gan River captured Taihe at the end of last month, and the burning and killing was extremely tragic. The Xiao bandits crossed the river and attempted to attack Ji'an, but were defeated by Deng's division, with more than 200 bandits killed. The electric wire mesh, artillery emplacements, pillboxes, and trenches newly built by Deng's division in Ji'an have now been completed, and the Nationalist and People's Rights ships are escorting the Ji'an to the provincial capital mail. The fortifications around the provincial capital were originally very solid, and Commander-in-Chief Lu is also planning to follow the Guangdong method of building pillboxes at various key points and setting up machine guns and cannons to consolidate the security of the provincial capital. (August 22nd)

The Legislative Yuan Passed 54

Regulations on the Business of Weights and Measures Instruments 55

The Legislative Yuan passed the following Regulations on the Business of Weights and Measures Instruments at its 106th meeting on the 23rd: (Article 1) Those who engage in the business of manufacturing, selling, or repairing weights and measures instruments shall apply to the local competent authority for a license, which shall be forwarded to the National Bureau of Weights and Measures for record. The aforementioned license shall be issued by the National Bureau of Weights and Measures for the use of the local competent authority. (Article 2) The validity period of a license for the business of weights and measures instruments shall be ten years, calculated from the date of issuance, but it may be renewed for another ten years upon application without paying a license fee. (Article 3) Applicants who engage in the manufacturing business shall pay the license fee in accordance with the following provisions: 1. Those who use motive power machinery and regularly employ 30 or more workers: 50 yuan. 2. Those who use motive power machinery and regularly employ less than 30 workers: 30 yuan. 3. Those who manufacture by hand and regularly employ 30 or more workers: 20 yuan. 4. Those who manufacture by hand and regularly employ 10 or more workers: 10 yuan. 5. Those who manufacture by hand and employ less than 10 workers: 5 yuan. (Article 4) Applicants who engage in the business of selling or repairing shall pay the license fee in accordance with the following provisions: 1. Sellers: 5 yuan. 2. Repairers: 2 yuan. (Article 5) Those who have a manufacturing license may concurrently engage in the business of selling and repairing. Those who have a selling license may concurrently engage in the business of repairing. (Article 6) Those who have a manufacturing license shall prepare to purchase standard instruments at a price. (Article 7) Those who have any of the following circumstances shall not engage in the business of weights and measures instruments: 1. Those who have committed any of the crimes stipulated in Chapter 13 of the Criminal Code and have been sentenced to punishment, and one year has not yet passed since the completion of the execution or remission of the execution. 2. Those whose licenses have been revoked or whose business has been suspended in accordance with Article 18 of the Weights and Measures Law or the provisions of these Regulations, and one year has not yet passed. (Article 8) Those who have obtained a license and commit any of the crimes stipulated in Chapter 13 of the Criminal Code shall have their license revoked upon being sentenced to punishment. (Article 9) These Regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Imminent Resumption of Shipping in Fuzhou 56

Business Sector Suffers Losses of Approximately Two Million

Fuzhou Correspondence: Since the outbreak of the war in Fujian Province, transportation between the provincial capital and northern Fujian has been severed, and commercial shipping has completely stagnated. Tea, rice, paper, bamboo, wood, bamboo shoots, and charcoal produced in northern Fujian have been stockpiled in the mountains and cannot be shipped downstream. Cloth, salt, oil, flour, hardware, and sundries from the provincial capital cannot be shipped upstream, leaving no way to provide supplies. As a result, commerce in both the provincial capital and northern Fujian is deteriorating daily, and bankruptcies are constantly heard, impacting Shanghai and Hong Kong trading houses that have established branches in Fujian to engage in import and export trade, leading to significant losses. It is estimated that business losses in the past two months have exceeded two million yuan. If this continues without relief measures, the financial situation at the end of the year will be dire. Currently, business circles in Fuzhou and Yanping, in order to save themselves, have jointly launched a movement to restore river transport. After much effort and appeals, they have obtained the understanding of local military authorities. The financial authorities, due to the decline in tax revenues after the suspension of freight transport, are particularly supportive. Yesterday, the 20th, the Fuzhou General Chamber of Commerce convened a meeting of import and export merchants to discuss resumption measures. The Provincial Government, the Finance Department, the Special Commissioner's Office, the 56th Division Headquarters, and the Marine

Page 12

Corps Headquarters all sent special commissioners to participate. The results of the discussions were quite satisfactory. The general plan is for the military authorities to establish an inspection station at Hongshan Bridge to specifically inspect goods shipped downstream from northern Fujian. On the northern Fujian side, the Yanping Chamber of Commerce will request local military authorities to establish an inspection station at Shuikou to specifically inspect goods shipped upstream from the provincial capital. If there is no contraband, they will be allowed to pass during the ceasefire period to facilitate circulation. Goods shipped upstream and downstream before the outbreak of hostilities that have been stranded at various bamboo rafts and other locations have already been specially released to prevent spoilage. They have arrived and are being unloaded one after another, awaiting clear procedures before being reloaded and shipped back. This is a glimmer of hope for the business community in Fujian Province. (August 21st)

The Jiaoji Railway After the Great War 57

Jinan Correspondence: Since the Jin army's eastward advance, the entire Jiaoji Railway line has almost entirely fallen into military zones, resulting in property losses and business deficits estimated at over two million yuan. With the recovery of Jinan by the Central Army and the rout of the Jin army, the railway has been cleared and reopened to traffic on the 19th. The extent of the damage to the railway and the Railway Bureau's preparations for reopening are summarized below: (1) Regarding bridges, there has been no major damage from Qingdao to Zuoshan. The most severe damage is between Zuoshan and Zihedian. Many bridges, such as the Wei River, Dawei River, Yun River, Xiaotang River, Zi River, Baiyang River, and nearby river bridges, were blown up by the Jin army. Some had one or two spans, others had five or six spans. The Railway Bureau sent the heads of the engineering and traffic departments to inspect and supervise repairs on the 12th of this month. All the destroyed bridges have now been temporarily repaired with sleeper-supported piers and can barely handle traffic. There is less damage west of Xindian to Jinan. (2) Regarding rolling stock, since the outbreak of hostilities, the Jin army detained approximately two hundred cars on the western section. The eastern section has approximately eighty locomotives belonging to this railway and other railways, approximately two hundred passenger cars, and approximately one thousand four hundred freight cars. Most are currently being used for military transport. The Jin army did not take the rolling stock on the western section when they retreated, thanks to negotiations with the Japanese side, which preserved them. (3) Regarding telegraphs and telephones, telegraph poles and electrical machinery along the line west of Zuoshan were mostly destroyed by the Jin army. Even telephone sets and batteries were mostly taken away, resulting in great losses. The Railway Bureau is gradually repairing the train dispatch telephones and route signs. However, there are extreme difficulties in obtaining workers and materials. The Railway Bureau is currently transporting existing materials to be used as much as possible and borrowing workers from the city telephone bureau in order to complete the repairs as soon as possible. (4) Fundamental plans: The Railway Bureau's repairs to the destroyed bridges this time were originally intended as an emergency measure, using sleeper-supported piers, which are inherently dangerous. To be cautious, the railway has specifically instructed all drivers to pay attention and proceed slowly when passing over the bridges and to assign craftsmen to guard each wooden pier to repair it at any time to avoid oversights. However, this is not a permanent solution. Therefore, the railway has instructed the engineering department to design detailed plans for fundamental repairs. For the destroyed bridges that were originally planned to be replaced or have alternate lines built, it is currently planned to allow traffic to pass on the alternate lines temporarily. Other bridges are also planned for fundamental repairs. However, iron plates and steel materials are needed. In addition to the materials originally purchased and stored by the railway, which can be transported for use, those that have been purchased but not yet delivered will be telegraphed separately to expedite delivery for continuous application. (5) Remedial measures: Salaries of the railway's east and west section employees are urgently needed to be reissued, and interest on debts, which amounts to more than 500,000 yuan per month, cannot be delayed. In the past month, with the interruption of traffic, the railway's operating revenue was only about one-tenth of what it used to be. It is now actively rushing to repair bridges in the shortest possible time. The large amounts of materials and funds required are huge. The Railway Bureau is digging everywhere to meet urgent needs, but it is still difficult. It is now planned to reduce and issue employee salaries in proportion to subsidize. It is reported that regulations stipulate that from this month, employee salaries of over one hundred yuan will be paid at 80% first. (August 21st)

Natural Disasters and Man-Made Calamities in Various Counties of Henan Province 58

Xingyang, Kaifeng Correspondence: According to someone who recently came from Xingyang, the fifth, sixth, seventh, eighth, and ninth districts of southern Xingyang are surrounded by mountains on three sides and have always been a haunt for bandits. This spring, a large band of bandits occupied the northern border of Mixian County, which is close to the seventh district of Xingyang. Consequently, more than three thousand bandits infiltrated from Fangguo and other villages in the south of the sixth district and occupied the fifth, sixth, and seventh districts, causing devastating burning and looting. It is estimated that more than forty li from north to south and fifty li from east to west in southern Xingyang are all under bandit control. More than five hundred villages in the area have been reduced to ashes. When the garrison led by Commander Li came to suppress them, the bandits fled again, pushing the captured elderly and weak into ditches and killing the disabled on the roads. Deaths and injuries were everywhere, and the mountains were filled with blood and flesh. Later investigations revealed that approximately 15,400 people were captured or injured, and approximately 9,600 houses were burned down. The loss of property and food is incalculable. Currently, the markets are deserted, and people are scarce. Corpses are exposed without anyone to collect them, and there is no strength to repair the burned houses. The captured have no money to redeem themselves, and the survivors have nowhere to return. It is truly an unprecedented disaster.

Neihuang: Li Shican of the Henan Provincial Relief Committee sent a telegram on the 8th to the Red Cross Society, the Red Swastika Society, the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association, and various charities in Beijing and Shanghai, stating that, according to reports from the Neihuang Relief Sub-Committee, Neihuang County is the poorest area in northern Henan, and has suffered from years of war and banditry, making life unbearable. In the 17th year, there was drought and locusts; in the 18th year, there were drought, floods, and locusts, three disasters occurring simultaneously. Tens of thousands of disaster victims abandoned their homes and went to the Northeast to seek food. This spring, they encountered another political upheaval, and the allocation of funds and conscription of soldiers exhausted everything. They hoped that the wheat harvest would save their lives, but unexpectedly, violent winds and hailstorms wreaked havoc, causing all the wheat ears to be broken and the harvest completely lost. The young autumn seedlings were also severely damaged, and the autumn harvest is also hopeless. The surviving people are dying and urgently need relief. Neihuang is a barren and impoverished area that has suffered from repeated disasters, resulting in depleted wealth and food. This time, it has suffered another severe wind and hail disaster, with the complete loss of wheat and grain, making it difficult to sustain life. They earnestly request all philanthropists to have great compassion and provide generous relief to save the disaster victims. They are deeply grateful.

Linru: Li Shican of the Henan Provincial Relief Committee sent a telegram on the 10th to Taiyuan, Zhengzhou, and Nanjing, stating that, according to reports from various organizations in Linru, bandit leader Cui Yinchuan and others captured Zhouzhuang Village in the northeast of the county, killing more than one hundred people, extorting more than one hundred tickets, looting property, and burning everything down. Duzhuang Village in the west of the county was captured by bandits, who are still occupying it. On July 15th, the west gate of the county seat was attacked by a large number of bandits, who burned, killed, looted, and caused incalculable losses. Before leaving, they kidnapped 158 tickets. On the night of July 18th, Shilibu, ten miles west of the city, was again attacked and looted by the bandits occupying Duzhuang Village, who burned everything down and kidnapped more than one hundred people. On the 28th, a village east of the city was also captured by bandits, with even more severe burning and killing, and even greater losses. Currently, bandits are everywhere in the fourth, sixth, and seventh districts south of the Ru River, and people find it difficult to escape. They cannot afford to redeem the kidnapped tickets, and the dying disaster victims are begging for relief. After investigating the villages affected in Linru, their wealth has been exhausted. If no measures are taken to provide relief, the lives of the people cannot be saved. He earnestly requests the swift allocation of relief funds to save the survivors, and eagerly awaits orders.

Russian Bandits Disturb the Eastern Railway 59

Three Incidents in Three Days

Secret Soviet Manipulation

Harbin Correspondence: The actions of Russian bandits on the Harbin-Manzhouli line have recently become completely disciplined, and their attempts to harm traffic on the western line are becoming increasingly urgent. On the evening of the 15th of this month, a large number of stacked sleepers were found on the railway tracks at Duiqingshan Station, one hundred li from Harbin. The 23rd passenger train from Harbin to Ang'angxi Station passed through the area at 12:50 a.m., but fortunately, they were discovered early, and the train was not derailed. This is one incident. At 2:00 a.m. on the 16th, several hundred Russian bandits invaded Bali Station between Boketu and Hailar. The local garrison of only a dozen soldiers was unable to resist, and the station was burned and looted by the bandits, who killed six Chinese workers and burned down the entire station before leaving. This is another incident. On the morning of the 17th, the fourth passenger train from Manzhouli to Harbin was approaching Shartu Station when it was discovered that someone had pushed a freight car onto the tracks in heavy fog, intending to cause a tragic train collision. Fortunately, the driver saw it and stopped the train in time, avoiding danger. In addition, there have been countless incidents of hollowing out sleepers and removing spikes. According to reports from the Railway Protection Army Headquarters, in addition to the Zhu Guofu gang, which ostensibly claims to be "anti-communist," the other gangs all have official Soviet officers inside. One of the most famous officers is "Gusya Yina Ali." These Russian bandits are stationed in various places and specialize in harassing small stations in remote areas with weak defenses. Their main base has advanced to the Yalu County border, in a forest. Recently, many Mongolians have joined, so the bandit forces are quite large. It was previously reported that the Russian director of the Eastern Railway, "Berzin," went to Boketu, ostensibly to meet with Russian bandit leaders. Although his intentions are unknown, it is likely to convey orders from the Russian cadres of the Eastern Railway. The Soviet Union's motivation for encouraging Russian bandits to harass the Eastern Railway line is said to be quite profound. The proposal to increase the number of Red Army troops stationed along the Eastern Railway line, which was raised at the Blagoveshchensk Conference, has not yet reached a clear conclusion. Now that the Sino-Russian Conference is in progress, the Russian side raised this matter again, but Mo Teh-hui rejected it in the preparatory meeting. Therefore, they are using a roundabout method, secretly instigating Russian bandits to disrupt the Eastern Railway line. Since the western region is vast and there are means of entering and exiting, they are wreaking havoc at an accelerating pace. These so-called Russian bandits have well-equipped guns and ammunition, suggesting that they are a disguised form of regular troops. In the future, if the western region is disrupted and uneasy, or a major terror occurs, the Russian side can use the excuse that the Chinese army is unable to protect the railway line and demand to increase the number of Soviet troops stationed there. Our side is aware of their hidden intentions. The 51st Regiment and 43rd Regiment of Su Bingwen's brigade of the Heilongjiang Army have each dispatched units on the 15th to pursue Russian bandits in the Solun and Yalu areas. The Railway Protection Army Headquarters is also planning to add armored train units to patrol the Harbin-Manzhouli line to prevent problems before they arise. (August 18th)

Zhalainuoer Coal Mine Problem 60

The Political Committee Has Ordered Restoration

The Board of Directors Holds an Extraordinary Meeting

Harbin Correspondence: The Eastern Railway Board of Directors will convene an extraordinary board meeting tomorrow to discuss the issue of the rise and fall of the Zhalainuoer Coal Mine, bringing together Chinese and Russian directors to discuss how to handle this issue. Since Mo Teh-hui's departure abroad, all matters related to the railway have been decided through consultations between the Chinese acting director Li Shaogeng and the Russian deputy director Yemushanav. Important matters, except for those that cannot be delayed, are implemented first and then submitted for retroactive recognition when a formal meeting is convened in the future. All other matters are suspended. Regarding the Zhalainuoer Coal Mine, the Russian Railway Bureau chief submitted a report last month stating that it is necessary to organize a miners' committee and explore the coal seams first. The opinions of Soviet cadres generally tend towards shutting it down and recommending that the Eastern Railway use Suicheng coal from Russia. Guan Yupu, director of the materials department of the Eastern Railway, and other department heads who care about the future of the Eastern Railway, believe that shutting down the Zhalainuoer Coal Mine is the Soviet Union's deliberate attempt to lead the Eastern Railway to suicide. Therefore, they petitioned the Northeast Political Affairs Committee to order the Eastern Railway authorities to restore it. The Political Committee then ordered the Chinese director to take charge of the matter. This matter is of such importance to our country. Therefore, after receiving the order, the Chinese authorities first contacted the Russian side to obtain their consent and convened an extraordinary meeting before the number of directors was complete to decide whether to restore the coal mine. At tomorrow's meeting, there will be three Chinese and three Russian directors in Harbin. Although it is not a formal meeting, there may be a debate. It is reported that the specific opinions of the Chinese side have been decided: regardless of what happens, one side must send personnel to explore the coal seams, and the other side must immediately hire workers to mine the areas where coal seams have already been discovered. If this is the case, it will violate the Russian side's intention to sell Soviet coal, which they may not want. As for the Eastern Railway's 1930 budget, it has already been reviewed by the board of directors. It was decided that the railway's income this year has sharply decreased on all lines, and each passenger and freight train is losing money. If income does not increase in the next few months, it will be necessary to borrow money to survive. Therefore, the opinions of the bureaus and departments are all willing to save money, reduce redundant personnel, streamline operations, and reduce all departmental budgets by 20%. The announced layoffs in various departments include more than 470 in the business department, more than 130 in the engineering department, more than 280 in the materials department, more than 90 in the machinery department, more than 20 in the general affairs department, and more than 30 in the land department. The total number is approximately 1,200, including more than 400 Chinese employees, more than 200 White Russians, and the rest are Soviets. However, it is said that the Russian personnel who are laid off all return to their home country, and at the same time, new personnel are investigated from their home country and appointed in their name to fill the positions. If this is the case, then only the Chinese employees and White Russians will be laid off. Although this statement is making a lot of noise in Harbin, it has not yet been seen in reality.

Wuhu Organizes a Party, Government, and Military Affairs Office 61

Wuhu Correspondence: Wuhu is located in the middle reaches of the Yangtze River and serves as a shield for the capital. At a time when military progress is being made on the front lines, the security of the rear is particularly important. Ma Fuxiang, chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, who has been staying in the capital for a long time, recently returned to Anhui after being urged by the central government. When Ma passed through Wuhu, he summoned the director of the Public Security Bureau, Tang Shaogao, and the magistrate of Wuhu County, Sun Gongming, to discuss the maintenance of local security. At the same time, the central government, considering that Wuhu is a mixed area of Chinese and foreigners and that reactionary elements can easily hide, has already dispatched Huang Geng to Wuhu yesterday to organize the Wuhu Postal and Telegraph Inspection Office for strict inspection. In addition, Xiong Wenxu, member of the Anhui Provincial Party Affairs Reorganization Committee and Minister of Propaganda, was ordered to come to Wuhu the day before yesterday to organize a joint party, government, and military affairs office in Wuhu to prevent reactionary elements. Xiong came to Wuhu and stayed at the Minguo Daily newspaper office, discussing the organizational law with various party and government agencies here for several days. The location is planned to be inside the Cloth Merchants' Guild, with separate secretarial, general affairs, and secret investigation groups. It has been decided to appoint five people as committee members: Provincial Propaganda Minister Xiong Wenxu, Wuhu Municipal Director Shao Yizhou, Public Security Bureau Director Tang Shaogao, County Magistrate Sun Gongming, and Sixth District Bandit Suppression Commander Lü Xueshu. The office will be declared established in one day. The expenses will be directly allocated by the province, and it is also planned to select outstanding members from the party members in the province to organize a propaganda team to go to various counties to propagate, so that the people can understand and assist in eradicating reactionaries. At an appropriate time, they will be dispatched to the bandit suppression command headquarters in various districts to carry out propaganda with the army. This measure will be implemented after the provincial government convenes a meeting of the bandit suppression commanders in various districts. (August 23rd)

Wuhu Express Mail 62

The Anhui Provincial Party Affairs Reorganization Committee telegraphed that the Seventh Standing Committee of the Provincial Reorganization Committee resolved that, in addition to the provincial agricultural association, the labor union, the women's association, and the Anqing labor and women's organizations, the Wuhu General Labor Union and other mass organizations should also be suspended and reorganized by dispatched personnel.

The Wuhu County government, in order to increase bandit prevention forces, prepared funds to purchase thirty rifles and five thousand rounds of ammunition from the Security Department of the provincial government. They have now arrived in the province. The county government yesterday sent Cui Chuqing as a representative to the province to collect and transport them. The General Chamber of Commerce here yesterday submitted a report to the Ministry of Communications, stating that the telephone poles and wires in Wuhu City have been decayed for a long time and often break and fall, causing fatal accidents. They earnestly request the Ministry to order the Wuhu City Telephone Bureau to quickly replace all decayed materials to maintain communication and ensure safety. Ma Fuxiang, chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, today accompanied Sun Shengwu, director of the Finance Department, on a river steamer from the capital to Wuhu to return to the province. (August 21st)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 63

A glimpse of rampant banditry in Jin County: Qianwei and Langxia in the neighboring Jinshan County have been areas where bandits frequently appear. Although the military and police have repeatedly suppressed them, they always hear the news in advance and flee, gathering and dispersing irregularly. Yesterday (the 22nd) at 1:00 p.m., more than one hundred bandits, armed with rifles and pistols, ravaged the three towns of Qianwei, Lüxiang, and Langxia, which is truly shocking to hear. This gang of bandits targeted Inspector Fei of Lüxiang because he was strict in investigating bandits, resulting in the bandits' anger. They sought revenge by robbing weapons and killing. They walked from Lüxiang and Langxia to Qianwei, surrounded the Public Security Bureau, robbed weapons, and then went to Lüxiang, where they again surrounded the local Public Security Station. Inspector Fei was the first to raise his gun and attack. One bandit was shot and seriously injured. The bandits fought Inspector Fei head-on. Fei was outnumbered and killed on the spot. The station's weapons were then robbed. This battle lasted several minutes. One gatekeeper was captured, and three policemen were injured. It is said that District Chief Jiang Lianjun was also killed. Six large boats docked in the river were all looted, including two pottery cargo ships, two bran ships, one oil tanker, and one rice ship, and six villagers were abducted as boatmen. Before leaving, they robbed drums and trumpets from the school and blew them away. Langxia Town was also affected. The police weapons were robbed, and all the wine jars piled up in the Hekang Sauce Garden in the town were smashed, using them as a source of amusement. The utensils in the home of store owner Zhu Liren were damaged, resulting in significant losses. Various places urgently notified the headquarters of the First Marine Police Team stationed in Songjiang by telephone. Captain Fan Guozhong was shocked by the news. In addition to reporting to the Minhang District Department, he immediately led more than ten naval vessels, towed by steamers, to the scene of the incident to search and pursue the bandits. In one day, they robbed three towns, robbed officials, and killed them, which is a first. It is truly a major robbery.

Airplane lands and damages itself after hitting a stone. A No. 19 aircraft encountered lightning and wind in the air the day before and was forced to land. However, the small training ground where it landed was too small, and the aircraft parts were accidentally damaged. Today, a Jiangyan aircraft flew to Songjiang to repair the No. 19 aircraft. The fuselage was also slightly damaged. Soon after, another Jiangyan aircraft drove to Songjiang. Currently, both the No. 19 and Jiangyan aircraft have driven to Shanghai, but the Jiangyang aircraft is still being repaired.

Another kidnapping case on the tidal mudflats of Fengjing. Yesterday (the 23rd) at about 5:00 a.m., a large band of bandits came to a place called Yibaoliutu in the tidal mudflats of Fengjing, riding on ten bandit ships. The bandits who landed numbered about sixty, and those who remained on the ships were also close to that number. They first looted four rifles from the area, fired a volley to demonstrate their power, and guarded the strategic passes. They broke into the home of village chief Xu Ruilin, looting wantonly and kidnapping the victim, Xu Ruilin, and taking him aboard the ship, demanding a ransom of 200,000. At the same time, the wife of the wealthy Wu Xiang, who was bedridden, was forced aboard the ship along with the ship and a boatman. Dai Jingru's son and the former head of the cabin, Wen, were also kidnapped because they had a feud with the bandits. In total, six people, including the boatman, were kidnapped. The Xu family suffered the greatest losses. After the looting, they sailed towards the Fanbang New Town area. A total of eleven ships, including the ship of the wealthy victim, were looted. The families of the victims were all at a loss. It is said that there were also reports of large-scale kidnappings in Zhangjingwan in Zhejiang Province. The rampant atmosphere of bandits can be seen.

The two kidnapped children of the Wang family have not yet escaped danger. The two children of the Wang family who were kidnapped in the Hougang kidnapping case are still in the bandit den. It is said that the Wang family received a letter from the bandits, but there was no news at the designated meeting place. The Wang family received another letter from the bandits the day before, accusing them of not being sincere in negotiating and threatening to burn down the entire town. This caused panic among the people in the town. However, the Wang family's financial situation has been strained in recent years, and it is difficult for them to raise the ransom demanded by the bandits. It is said that they have entrusted people to search everywhere to comfort the old mother who is looking forward to their return.

Suzhou 64

Wounded soldiers cured and sent to Beijing to return to their teams. Yesterday (the 24th), more than 240 wounded soldiers from the 15th Rear Hospital were discharged and sent to Beijing to return to their teams. When the train left at about 9:00 a.m., more than 50 people at the station refused to go to Beijing and asked to be sent to Shanghai instead. The rest disembarked when the train passed through Huguan. The 4th Regiment of the local military police heard the news and has dispatched a team to Huguan to arrest them. In addition, the perpetrator who injured the member of the defense corps with a gun in the Huqiu Garden was identified by the defense corps leader Ji Tianren yesterday and handed over to the inspection office for interrogation. A pistol was also found.

Wuxi 65

Progress on Establishing the County Court: The matter of establishing a county court in Xiyi (Wuxi) has, since the resolution of the court's location (the old Wuxi government office), been repeatedly addressed by the Higher Court, which dispatched Yao Guozhang, chief secretary of the Higher Court's prison section and preparatory officer for the county court, and Wang Yiming, secretary of the First Civil Tribunal, to Wuxi to design the court and raise establishment funds. Former County Magistrate Sun convened a meeting of various sectors to decide that the County Chamber of Commerce would subscribe 9,000 yuan and the Judicial Advancement Association would subscribe 2,000 yuan, to be paid in three installments. The 31st of this month is the deadline for the first installment. Higher Court President Lin, recognizing the urgency, especially dispatched Yao Guozhang and Jiang Yiming to Wuxi yesterday morning to negotiate the fundraising matters.

After disembarking, they immediately visited County Magistrate Pan, and then went to the Chamber of Commerce and the Judicial Advancement Association for discussions. The County Chamber of Commerce indicated that due to fundraising difficulties, the amount of 3,000 yuan for this installment might be difficult to approve. The Judicial Advancement Association agreed to pay the 1,000 yuan in full by the end of the month. At 5 p.m., Yao and Wang visited the county prison, detention center, and sub-detention center to inspect the inmates. They inquired in detail about the current state of the prison.

Suicide by Poisoning After Failed Loan Attempt: Qian Shaoqing, the 43-year-old owner of a water chestnut cake shop on Guanqian Street in the city, has recently been struggling due to slow business, causing him to borrow 100 silver dollars from his cousin Qian Zhuxuan, the owner of the Tongji Chun herbal medicine shop outside Guangfu Gate on Tongyun Road. Zhuxuan refused. Recently, he went to borrow again, but Zhuxuan happened to be in Shanghai on business. Shaoqing followed him to Shanghai. However, after arriving in Shanghai, Zhuxuan turned against him, refusing to acknowledge Shaoqing as his brother and calling the police to take Shaoqing to the police station, where he was fined 15 yuan. Shaoqing managed to raise the fine by the day before yesterday and was released by the police. He returned to Wuxi by car. Because of the failed loan and the police fine, he felt resentful and developed a desire to end his life. Yesterday at noon, he bought two yuan's worth of raw opium. At 6 p.m., he went to the Tongji Chun herbal medicine shop and sat silently. Qian Zhuxuan saw that he was weak and behaving strangely, and realized that he had taken poison. He rushed him to the Brothers Hospital for treatment, but his throat was already damaged and he could not be saved. At this time, Qian Shaoqing's sister, Lu Qian, and his sons, Jin Gen (17 years old) and Hai Gen (5 years old), had all arrived upon hearing the news. They ordered people to carry Shaoqing back to Zhuxuan's shop, where he died around 8 p.m., bleeding profusely from his nostrils. The scene was tragic. That night, Qian Zhuxuan and the head of the Tian San Tu district, Xi Zhiliang, reported to the county government. The county government, upon receiving the report, dispatched a trial officer and a Shen forensic officer on the morning of the 24th to conduct an autopsy. However, the family of the deceased has also made serious representations to Qian Zhuxuan, and it remains to be seen how this will be resolved.

Half-Day Strike at Qiantai Silk Factory: The Qiantai Silk Factory, located under the Gongyun Bridge on Liangxi Road outside Guangfu Gate, is solely owned by Cheng Bingruo of Wuxi and is generally doing well. However, its treatment of its workers is unusually strict, causing dissatisfaction among the female workers. The day before yesterday, the factory criticized the female workers for uneven silk thread, believing that if the work was not good, they should be guided instead of being reprimanded, which made them very angry. Yesterday morning (the 24th), a portion of the female workers went on strike, refusing to enter the factory to work and demanding improved treatment. Upon seeing this, the factory immediately reported to the Silk Factory Workers' Union, which dispatched officials such as Ding Shaochu to the factory to mediate with the factory's union official Wang Zengdi. A resolution was reached by noon, and the female workers agreed to return to work as usual this morning. The factory only works half a day in the morning due to the recent hot weather and stops working in the afternoon.

Changzhou 66

Gangsters Kill Each Other in the Northern Countryside: In the area of Lao Gu Bridge and Anjia She in the northern countryside of Wuyi County, gangsters are rampant. Villagers dare not only not speak of the gangsters, but also dare not travel during the day. Extortion and brutal killings are common. A villager named Liu recently received a gangster note demanding 1,000 yuan. After speaking to Bao Gen, who was associated with the gangsters, the matter was settled for 300 yuan. After the money was paid, Bao deducted 100 yuan and gave 200 yuan to the gangster leader. The gangster leader found out and was furious. He led the gangsters to Bao's house and searched it, finding several hundred yuan. Bao had been profiting from the situation more than once. The gangster leader immediately took Bao Fugen to Lao Gu Bridge and shot him dead. At the same time, a gangster named Xi Shunhai from Jiangyin was also shot for violating the rules of the gang. The families of the two gangsters went to collect their bodies yesterday morning (the 22nd) and prepared coffins for burial.

The Finance Bureau Takes Over the Fishery Tax Collection Office: The affairs of the Wuyi County fishery tax collection were previously handled by a collection office headed by Su Shaoquan. Now, Finance Bureau Director Liu has been ordered to take over the matter. In addition to ordering the former collector to hand over the office, he has appointed Wu Menglong, an official from the bureau, as the director of the collection office to handle all matters. The Higher Court Sends Personnel to Withdraw Funds: The Jiangsu Higher Court's expenses, allocated by the Finance Department, were 5,000 yuan from the Wujin Finance Bureau. On the 22nd, Higher Court President Lin specially sent Secretary Liu Zhixi to Changzhou to withdraw the funds. The Finance Bureau, citing limited surplus funds, paid 500 yuan first and will pay the rest at a later date.

His vacancy will be filled by Zhang Hongjun, the director of the Qidong Construction Bureau, which has already been abolished. Huang, the director of the Baoshan County Construction Bureau, has also been ordered to be transferred to the province for other appointments. His vacancy will be filled by Qian Tianhe, a technician from the department. The county magistrates of the two counties have been ordered to supervise the handover in accordance with regulations and report the results within the time limit.

The Principal of Suqian Middle School Comes to the Province to Appeal: Xiao Mingqin, the principal of the Jiangsu Provincial Suqian Middle School, recently received a payment order from the Education Department and withdrew over 1,000 yuan in cash from the Bank of China to return to the school. As he passed through Qingjiang, he was stopped by the troops stationed in the 266th district and falsely accused of being a bandit. He was taken to the city tower, bound with ropes, severely beaten, and paraded through the streets. The more than 1,000 yuan of school funds he was carrying were also lost at this time. After being driven out, he came to the province yesterday and presented his case to the Director of Education, requesting an investigation. Director Chen, after receiving the report, agreed to submit it to the Provincial Government for instructions.

Convening a Meeting of Rice Merchants to Stabilize Prices: Recently, new grains from various places have gradually entered the market, and rice prices have been easing daily. However, prices in Zhenjiang remain high. For the sake of the people's food supply, the County Party Department specially submitted a resolution to the County Government, requesting that rice merchants be convened to discuss ways to stabilize prices.

Nanjing 68

The Buddhist Layman's Forest is Established: Recently, local residents of Nanjing Zhu Tongsheng, Sun Huifeng, and Gan Gongsan believe that the capital city is a gathering place for talent, and Buddhist studies are a profound and subtle path. People in Europe and the United States are paying close attention to research, in order to advance in the realm of spiritual civilization. Therefore, they gathered like-minded individuals at Sifangcheng, behind Shiguanyin, in the eastern part of the city to organize the Nanjing Buddhist Layman's Forest. The official establishment meeting was held on August 3. All organizational outlines follow the methods of the Shanghai World Buddhist Layman's Forest. Many scholars from the capital attended the meeting. It was also decided that from August 17, the Great Master Yuexi of Yunnan would be invited to give a lecture on the entire Diamond Sutra and the entire Heart Sutra, as well as philosophy of life, etc., until September 6. Yesterday was the first day. Despite the heavy rain, there was still great enthusiasm. It is said that after this, there will also be a memorial service for the soldiers who died in the Northern and Southern wars, reciting the Liang Emperor's Repentance and the Earth Treasury Sutra until the birthday of the Earth Treasury Bodhisattva.

Yangzhou 69

The Cause and Effect of the Market Strike in Xianzhen: The market strike by various shops in Xianzhen, a town under the jurisdiction of Yangzhou, was resolved on the 22nd. The main reason for the strike was that Dong Yan Pingqing and others, who were involved in the rice business in the town, saw that the Sanyuan Bridge was collapsing and the ferry was dangerous. They convened merchants from various industries at the Dasheng Temple to discuss raising funds to build a pontoon bridge. However, Director Zhang of the Public Security Fourth Sub-bureau, listening to biased reports, led police to the temple to search for gambling and opium, without any evidence. He arrested Yan and others. The public was outraged and refused to open the market until they were released. However, the sub-bureau director then reported to the Public Security Bureau that they were obstructing official duties and requested that the Public Security Bureau send armed police and Inspector Dai to investigate and arrest Yan and others. This led to a public market closure. Fortunately, the Director of the Public Security Bureau learned the truth, transferred the police back, and ordered the release of the detainees. The Chamber of Commerce then issued a notice that the entire town would reopen the market.

The Shocking News of Pawned Bombs: At about 10 a.m. on the 23rd, several people brought bombs to the Dunjin pawnshop to pawn them, asking for 50 yuan for each. Fortunately, the clerk was quick-witted and pretended to negotiate the price, while secretly sending someone to alert the police. The joint military and police inspection office rushed to the scene and arrested five people, who were tied up and taken to the office for interrogation.

District Head Accused and Thoroughly Investigated: Min Jian, the head of the 12th district of this county, was previously accused by citizens such as Tu Jinbiao in a petition to the county government of privately collecting wheat donations and abusing local bullies such as Wang Huan as assistants. It is now heard that County Magistrate Wang has appointed Shi Shu to conduct a thorough investigation.

Robbery Case in the 12th District: The family of Wang Gui, a farmer in the 12th district of this county, was suddenly visited by more than ten bandits armed with guns the night before last. They broke down the door and entered, tied up the homeowner Wang Gui, and burned his breasts with fire, forcing him to reveal the location of his hidden silver. Wang, unable to bear the pain, revealed the location of the hidden silver, and more than 2,000 silver dollars were robbed. Before leaving, they also tied up his wife and two sons.

Qingpu 71

The District Warden Wrongfully Accused: Huang Suiliang, a resident of the second district of Qingpu County, previously mediated the case of Zhang Asi, an apprentice at Lu Yonggen's butcher shop, who fell into the river and drowned. Lu prepared a coffin for burial and paid the family of the deceased 180 yuan. Five people, including the anonymously-named butcher Hu Bin, falsely accused Huang Suiliang of being a local tyrant colluding with Wang Shixiu, coercing the family of the deceased, and privately settling the murder. The Ministry of Civil Affairs rejected the accusation. Hu Bin and others then appealed to the Higher Court. The Higher Court ordered the County Government to investigate and reply. It is now learned that the County Government has dispatched personnel to conduct a thorough investigation and found that the accusation was indeed false and that Hu Bin and others did not exist.

The County Magistrate Retakes the Oath: Yu Ding, the newly appointed County Magistrate of Qingpu, retook the oath of office in the Zhongshan Hall of the County Government the day before yesterday. Nantong 72

Burning the Bandit's Fake Headquarters: A large group of bandits is entrenched at the junction of Nantong and Rugao counties. The bandits have been routed after being suppressed by the military and police. The fake headquarters set up in Yingfanggang was searched, and many weapons and reactionary documents were seized. The bandits all fled. It was immediately set on fire and destroyed.

Requesting Disaster Relief for Coastal Floods: The riverbank from Yaogang to Shangang in Tongyi County has been eroded by more than 100 zhang this year due to repeated tidal surges. The embankment has collapsed, resulting in a severe tidal disaster. The County Government believes that the local financial resources can only be used for emergency rescue projects. It has specially presented a report to the Provincial Civil Affairs Department and the Provincial Relief Committee, requesting the allocation of funds to carry out the construction of revetment stone projects in exchange for labor.

Wounded Soldiers Will Soon Return to Their Units: More than half of the officers and soldiers who have recovered from their injuries at the 31st Rear Hospital recently will return to their units. The Commander-in-Chief has specially sent a committee to Tongzhou to count and verify them and issue certificates for their return to the units. These procedures are currently being prepared.

Jiashan 73

Bandits Kidnap People and Seize Weapons: At 7 a.m. on the 23rd, more than 100 bandits suddenly appeared in the tidal flats town on the border of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, kidnapping six people, including three villagers, who were released at the time. Xu Shaozhai's son Ruilin, Dai Jingru's son, and Deng were kidnapped, and two boxes of cannons from the security team were seized. At about 4 a.m. on the 23rd, the firearms of the official anti-smuggling team stationed in Zhangjinghui Town were also seized. In total, 24 rifles were seized from the commercial anti-smuggling team, 11 rifles were seized from the official anti-smuggling team, and 2 rifles were seized from the security team. After seizing the weapons, the bandits fled in the direction of Qianjingtang. The security team stationed in Shanxi pursued and suppressed them, but the bandits had already fled far away.

Conflict Caused by Injured Soldiers: At about 7 p.m. on the 23rd, the injured soldiers stationed in Shanxi suddenly swarmed into the city for unknown reasons and clashed with the security team stationed in Shanxi. The security team, seeing that the number of injured soldiers was quite large and difficult to stop, had no choice but to use live ammunition to guard them and telegraphed Hezhou to send a team to Shanxi on the night train to assist. The injured soldiers, seeing that they were no match for the security team, dispersed. More than ten people were injured, and more than ten people were arrested, including two who were seriously injured. All the shops and residents in the county were terrified when they heard the gunshots. Fortunately, it was quickly calmed down and did not cause a major disaster.

Pinghu 74

The Xinminxin Steamer Hijacked En Route: The Xinminxin steamer, which runs from Pinghu to Shanghai, was hijacked by seven or eight bandit boats yesterday (the 22nd) while traveling on the Xuputang River from Shanghai. The bandits ordered the steamer to stop, and the bandits swarmed onto the boat. All the passengers were searched. Fortunately, there were no major losses, and only scattered items were stolen. After a while, they left.

A Large Number of Refugees Arrive in Sigucun: At noon on the 21st, a large number of refugees, more than 300 people, arrived in Sigucun, Sigucqiao area. The local authorities reported it to the water police, who dispatched land and water police from the city to suppress it at 2 p.m. In the morning of the 22nd at 7am, they travelled towards Zhapu.

Banditry Rampant in the Eastern Countryside: Banditry is rampant in the eastern countryside, and extortion is a daily occurrence. Rumors have been spreading in Xincun Town recently, and residents are moving away, causing great panic. It seems that a great disaster is imminent. It is learned that bandit leader Taibao Ashu has led more than 400 of his men back to his old nest and has joined forces with various gangs, entrenched in Liujiawan Bridge and other places. They are quite rampant. Late at night on the 21st, it was suddenly reported that bandits were already in Yaan, and there was a secret arrival in the town. The situation suddenly became serious. The Public Security Bureau and the Provincial Security Team, upon hearing this, immediately dispatched a team of police to search. They first went to the home of Li Arong at Baoben Bridge, as Li was a relative of the notorious bandit Zhu Luo Amei. The inspection yielded nothing. However, Arong's son was seen escaping on the roof and was immediately taken back to the company headquarters by the team police. They then went to the home of Liu San, a former police officer in Jiangjiawei, but found no traces. It is heard that Li has also been released on bail.

Huzhou 75

Robbery and Kidnapping in Dongqiao Village: There are more than a dozen shops in Dongqiao Village, near Zhili Town in the northeastern countryside of this city. At about 6 p.m. on the 18th of this month, two bandit boats suddenly arrived. More than ten bandits with a Chaohu accent landed, fired their guns as a warning, and then looted. The Longhua and Tiansheng grain shops were robbed of more than 200 silver dollars. Ye Zhihe, the owner of Longhua, and Ye Shanting, the owner of Tiansheng, were kidnapped, and a resident named Liu was shot and injured. The whereabouts of the kidnapped people are still unknown.

Former Village Head of Qianzhi Village Shot Dead by Bandits: Qian Housheng, the village head of Qianzhi Village in Changxing County, had a modest family fortune and was coveted by bandits. Because the bandit atmosphere in that area was becoming increasingly intense, Qian Chun moved to the city. However, with the autumn harvest approaching, he returned to his hometown with his family on the 17th. Unexpectedly, at about 8 p.m. that night, more than ten bandits with a Henan accent, armed with guns, knives, and sticks, swarmed into his house. They did not rob anything, but dragged Qian Xiasheng out and shot him more than ten times before fleeing. Afterwards, Qian's family went out to check and found that Qian had died miserably on the ground. It is said that the reason for his death was that Qian had captured several bandits when he organized a self-defense group last year, so it was revenge.

Hangzhou 76

Corrupt Officials Tried Together: Zhang Jingzhi, an officer of the Zhejiang Civil Affairs Department, Zhou Jinying, a clerk of the Second District and Second Branch of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, and Fu Sanhe, a platoon leader of the anti-smuggling camp at Jianggan Zhaikou, were all found to have engaged in corruption. They were ordered to be dismissed from their posts and handed over to the Hangzhou County Local Court for separate punishment.

Construction Paid for with Debt and Treasury Bonds: Zhejiang Province was supposed to raise 2.5 million yuan in customs duty treasury bonds. The Finance Department believes that the province's finances are exhausted and the people can hardly bear the burden, while the military needs in the front are as urgent as a burning fire. There is really no solution at the moment. After repeated planning, the department intends to allocate the central government 10 million yuan of construction public bonds in the province to meet emergency needs.

Bandits Surround Linhai: Bandits in Linhai, Zhejiang Province, had their momentum somewhat suppressed after the troops stationed there launched a campaign to suppress them. Unexpectedly, they recently joined forces with bandits from Xianju, totaling more than 2,000 people, and surrounded Zhangjiadu Town in the western countryside of Linhai at night, pressing in from three sides. Fortunately, the military and civilians were prepared and defended together, fighting fiercely all night before the bandits collapsed.

Taizhou 77

Five Villages Jointly Organize a Security Team: The five villages of Datian, Xia Sha, and others in the eastern countryside of Linhai are now gathering local people to jointly organize a five-village joint security team because bandits are rising up in various villages. They will recruit 20 team soldiers to be stationed in Datian Town in this village for self-defense. The expenses will be borne by the local authorities, and they are actively proceeding with the project, which will soon be established.

Banditry Rampant in Zhangjiadu: Zhangjiadu in the western countryside of Linhai is the gateway to the northwestern countryside of this county. Since the bandits' riots in March of this year, the core area has been stationed with five regiments, two battalions, and six companies of soldiers and two platoons to defend it. Unexpectedly, at 4 a.m. the day before yesterday, more than 600 bandits suddenly arrived, hoping to seize the firearms of the soldiers of the company. Fortunately, the soldiers of the company joined forces with the local security team and launched a fierce attack, killing 11 bandits and wounding more than 50. The bandits were unable to withstand the attack and fled to Shangpingxiao in the same village.

Hefei 78

Fierce Battle Between Soldiers and Bandits in Gao Liuji: The 500-600 bandits of Huang Huiming, entrenched in Gao Liuji on the border of He and Shou counties, were severely suppressed by the 2nd and 3rd teams of the county self-defense force and the northwest brigades on the 15th, with dozens killed. After bandit leader Zhang Haifang was killed, they gathered other gangs on the 17th to counterattack. The soldiers fought back until night and killed the young bandit leader Kong Xiangxing. Chen Huaishan, a member of the county self-defense force, was also killed in battle. Upon hearing the news, Wang Shencheng, the head of the county self-defense force, personally led the first team and the artillery team to assist in the suppression on the morning of the 18th.

Political Program of the Chinese Nationalist Party 79

The Chinese Nationalist Party leads the national revolution to seek freedom and equality for China.

·········

The nationalism of the Nationalist Party has two aspects: first, the Chinese nation seeks its own liberation; second, all ethnic groups within China are equal.

··········

In addition to indirect civil rights, the Nationalist Party also implements direct civil rights (the rights of initiative, referendum, and recall).

··········

The most important principles of the Nationalist Party's livelihood are nothing more than two: (Equalization of Land Ownership) and (Regulation of Capital).

··········

First article of foreign policy: China recognizes as most-favored nations all countries that voluntarily renounce all privileges and are willing to abolish treaties that undermine China's sovereignty.

···········

Second article of domestic policy: The county is determined to be an autonomous unit. The people of an autonomous county have the right to directly elect and remove officials, and have the right to directly initiate and decide laws.

Joint Meeting of Various Institutions in Songbao 85

Report on Rampant Pirates in the Outer Waters of Songkou

At 10:00 AM yesterday, various institutions in Wusong, Baoshan, and Jiangwan held a joint meeting at the Wusong Chamber of Commerce. Representatives from the Fifth Division Supplementary Regiment, Wusong Chamber of Commerce, Defense Corps, Seventh District Public Security Bureau, Baoshan County Government, County Public Security Bureau, Seventh District Party Headquarters, Fourth District Water Police, and Water Patrol Team attended. Yu Zhen presided over the meeting. Representatives from the Baoshan County Government and the Fourth District Water Police successively reported on the rampant pirates in the outer waters of Wusongkou. In general, it was said that Qidong Lvsisha outside Songkou is surrounded by water on all sides, with an island in the middle, covering about dozens of miles. There are 70 to 80 pirate ships parked in the sand, with more than 600 pirates. In addition, there are more than 100 pirate ships and about 1,000 pirates in Da'an Port, Haimen. They are fully armed and very well-equipped, and their organization is also very strict. According to the above-mentioned sandbanks, they are all shoals, and warships cannot enter, and the army is also out of reach. Therefore, these pirates are becoming increasingly rampant, either kidnapping ships for ransom or landing to loot, almost every day. If we want to thoroughly suppress them, we must advance by both land and sea to eliminate them. After discussion, it was decided to investigate the terrain of the sandbank and the details of the port, and then conduct a joint land and sea suppression.

Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance Rectifies Autumn Survey 86

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance believes that the autumn surveys of disasters and crop failures in various counties of the province are often falsely reported. Now that the autumn survey period is approaching, in order to rectify the situation, the Autumn Survey Regulations have been specially formulated, and the deadline for submitting autumn survey reports from various counties has been stipulated, instructing everyone to comply. The deadline for Shanghai County is the end of September, and it will be invalid if it is overdue. Therefore, after receiving the order, Magistrate Yan, in addition to notifying the Finance Bureau, yesterday also copied the regulations and instructed all districts to comply without violation.

Red Cross Revises Bylaws Committee 87

Second Meeting

The Red Cross Bylaws Revision Committee held its second meeting at 2:00 PM on the 23rd of this month. The committee members present included Wen Lanting, Li Zhenbang, Hong Yanbin, Ye Zhisheng, Wang Peiyuan, Xu Xichun, Xue Shaoting, Dong Xinqin, Wang Xiaolai, and Liu Hongsheng. The meeting passed the association's operating rules established by Ye Zhisheng. The chairman proposed to revise the bylaws of the Chinese Red Cross. After joint discussion and item-by-item research, the first article of the first chapter to the twenty-fifth article of the fourth chapter were all revised and passed. Because it was late, the rest will be discussed at the next meeting. The operating rules are listed below. The simplified charter and operating rules of the Bylaws Revision Committee of the Third Temporary Congress of the Chinese Red Cross: Article 1, Name: This committee is produced by the Third Temporary Congress, so it is named the Bylaws Revision Committee of the Third Temporary Congress. Article 2, Purpose: The purpose of this committee is to revise all bylaws of the Chinese Red Cross. Article 3, Organization: This committee is organized by 31 people publicly recommended by the Third Temporary Congress. There is also one chairman, who is elected from the 11 people. Article 4, Powers: All members of this committee are purely voluntary and have the power to revise all bylaws of the Chinese Red Cross. Article 5, Meetings: Each meeting of this committee is convened by the elected chairman. The time is determined by the chairman. Article 6, Meeting: This committee only discusses the revision of bylaws and does not discuss other matters. During the meeting, if it is necessary to revise a certain article or item, it should be proposed by one person and seconded by two people before it can be moved. It can be voted on after it is passed by more than half of the members present. Article 7, Quorum: More than half of the members constitute a quorum. Article 8, Term of Office: The term of office of this committee is until the revision of the bylaws is completed, submitted to the Standing Committee, and submitted to the National Government for record. Article 9, Responsibility: Each member of this committee, having been publicly recommended, should bear a part of the responsibility and should attend each meeting on time and not be absent on any pretext, so as not to hinder the progress of the association's affairs.
