Xiong Shihui Mourns the Deceased 88

Madam Gu Zhuzhen Passed Away Yesterday Morning

Madam Gu Zhuzhen, wife of Xiong Shihui, Commander of the Shanghai-Wusong Garrison,

Contracted typhoid fever in the middle of this month and was admitted to Fumin Hospital for diagnosis and treatment. The medicine was ineffective, and she passed away at 7:30 AM yesterday morning. It is said that when the illness first started, she only felt slightly unwell. Because she had received a preventive injection for typhoid fever before, she did not suspect that it was this disease at first. Commander Xiong was also busy with official duties and did not pay much attention. After returning from inspecting the Shanghai-Hangzhou line, he ordered her to be admitted to the hospital. At this time, the condition was still not very serious, but the disease was malignant. After being admitted to the hospital for several days, she fell into a coma due to excessive fever, coupled with heart failure, which eventually led to her death. Madam was from Zhuji, Zhejiang Province, and was the eldest daughter of Mr. Gu Zitong, a retired lieutenant general and advisor to the Military Advisory Council. She graduated from Tokyo Women's Medical College. After her death, her body was moved to the Universal Funeral Home on Jiaozhou Road and is scheduled to be encoffined at 4:00 PM today. It is said that it will be temporarily stored there.

Coal Merchants Oppose Mandatory Levy of Treasury Bonds 92

The Shanghai Coal Industry Association, regarding the Coal Special Tax Bureau's mandatory levy of 20% of treasury bonds, sent five representatives to the Municipal Government and the Municipal Party Headquarters yesterday to petition and present receipts. Now, they have filed a series of appeals. The text of their petition is recorded as follows: "Presented to maintain order and prevent problems, please uphold justice. Since the Jiangsu Provincial Coal Special Tax Bureau implemented the mandatory levy of 20% of cigarette treasury bonds along with taxes on August 10th, actively forcing the collection, making the coal merchants, who are already suffering, almost driven to their deaths. Therefore, the public's feelings are indignant, as if a great disaster is about to come. The executive committee of the association has repeatedly advocated for a peaceful and legal opposition, advocating that the bureau be given the opportunity to automatically revoke the mandatory levy by September 5th. By that date, the bureau still could not resolve the issue. In accordance with the unanimous public opinion of the industry, they refused to pay the 20% cigarette treasury bonds levied along with taxes, which has been announced in the newspaper. It is feared that the bureau will still not cancel the levy by the deadline, and the coal merchants will inevitably refuse to pay. Under these circumstances, the bureau may use the name of tax resistance to enforce ship detention. Once the ships are detained, the coal merchants will inevitably be forced to suspend operations. If so, transportation and factories will inevitably be suspended, affecting the rear of the war and local order, which is by no means insignificant. If it unfortunately comes to this state, the responsibility should be borne by the Coal Special Tax Bureau. In order to prevent problems, the association hereby clarifies and respectfully requests your department to uphold justice and forward the matter to the Municipal Government and the Water and Land Public Security Bureau, so as not to assist in the detention of ships, so as to avoid trouble in the rear. The Shanghai Special Municipal Party Headquarters and the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau."

Foreign Merchants Monopolize the Tianjin Cigarette Industry 93

Chinese Merchants Request Negotiation with the Consolidated Tax Bureau

The Cigarette Consolidated Tax Bureau of the Ministry of Finance, in order to cut off the source of cigarette tax in Hebei, has stopped issuing transportation permits for cigarette shipments to Hebei from today to show its resistance, as reported in this newspaper. It is now known that the Chinese Cigarette Factory Trade Association has repeatedly received letters and telegrams from members reporting that although the British-American Tobacco Company in Tianjin has taken the step of closing its factory to resist taxes, more than 20,000 boxes of cigarettes in its foreign warehouses have been secretly reported for tax payment by various managers and are being widely sold. At present, the area under the jurisdiction of Hebei has become a monopoly area for the British-American Tobacco Company, while Chinese cigarettes have been out of stock for more than ten days since the shutdown. There is still no news of lifting the ban, creating an excellent opportunity for foreign merchants. If the period is extended, business is worrying and solutions should be found. After receiving the report, the association immediately retrieved the original letters and telegrams from various companies in Tianjin and knew that the matter was true and was very angry. The foreign company is taking advantage of the situation, obeying superficially but disobeying secretly, indirectly undermining the bureau's orders and directly monopolizing the business. There could be no more improper competition. It is said that representatives have been publicly elected to inquire about solutions from the Cigarette Consolidated Tax Bureau of the Ministry of Finance. The following is a telegram from Tianjin: "It is found that the British-American Tobacco Company in Tianjin has more than 20,000 boxes of inventory. The managers are now paying the new tax. This transitional measure is obedient superficially but disobedient secretly, and Chinese merchants are sitting and waiting for death. The association should come forward and negotiate seriously with the tax bureau."

Products of the Provincial Agricultural Implement Manufacturing Institute 94

Tax-Free Nationwide

The Jiangsu Provincial Agricultural Implement Manufacturing Institute in Suzhou is currently the only government-run agricultural implement manufacturing institution in China. Its diesel engines, kerosene engines, centrifugal pumps, rice milling machines, cultivators, new-style plows, row planters, etc., are well-made and low-priced. They have long been popular in various counties of the province. Agricultural institutions and farmers in other provinces, such as Henan, Hubei, Sichuan, Hunan, Jiangxi, Fujian, Zhejiang, and Anhui, have also come to Suzhou from afar to purchase them to promote and popularize them. However, the products of the institute were already exempt from tax in the province with the special permission of the Ministry of Finance, but when they were transported out of the province, they still had to pay taxes, which was very expensive. Foreign provinces often hesitated because of this. The institute, in view of the decline of agriculture in China in recent years, and the improvement of agricultural implements cannot be delayed, and before the central government and various provinces have specially established agricultural implement manufacturing institutes, it is not appropriate to have regionalism for the needs of foreign provinces and to have discrimination. Therefore, it specially requested the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mining to forward the request to the Ministry of Finance, requiring that the products of the institute be tax-free nationwide. The Ministry of Finance has now approved it and has replied to the provincial government, saying, "This case was previously approved and forwarded to the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, the Jiangsu Finance Special Envoy, and the Jiangsu Customs Superintendent, allowing tax exemption. This time, the request to order the financial departments, financial special envoys, and customs superintendents of various provinces to allow tax exemption nationwide is approved in order to promote agriculture in various provinces. In the future, the products of the institute can be tax-free nationwide, and both near and far can benefit from this tax exemption for agricultural implements, which will greatly benefit the promotion of new agricultural implements."

Inspection of Jiangbei Wheat Stopped 95

The Jiangbei Branch of the Shanghai Agricultural Products Inspection Institute of the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining began inspection in Gaoyou on the 17th of this month. On that day, more than 300 ships transporting wheat arrived at Gaoyou Hexia. It took the institute two hours to inspect the wheat on one ship. The results of the inspection on that day showed that only one-tenth had been inspected. Feeling that the procedures were difficult and difficult to handle, the director of the branch went to the Wheat Merchants Association in person and stated that there was no room for accommodation in the handling procedures. In the future, when the wheat shops receive wheat, if they encounter wheat mixed with water and mud, they will hand it over to the branch for processing. Now, the branch has voluntarily stopped inspection. Regarding the opposition of domestic manufacturers to paying the inspection fee, they agreed to record it on the books and not pay it temporarily to show leniency. In fact, domestic flour mills are located in the wheat-producing areas, and they purchase raw materials at a loss. There is no reason to buy inferior goods. Shanghai manufacturers initially intended to request the Department of Civil Affairs to issue a strict ban in various counties of Jiangbei due to the occasional occurrence of water and mud mixing by wheat transport ships. Now that the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining has established an institute for inspection, it is indeed an urgent task to inspect and improve the quality of wheat in the hands of farmers. However, because it is abandoning the fundamentals and pursuing the trivial, and the handling is difficult, Shanghai manufacturers have felt that they have lost the original intention of their request.

Reasons for the Late Arrival of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Night Express Train the Night Before Last 96

Disturbances by Wounded Soldiers in Jiashan Quickly Suppressed

The 34th Rear Hospital of the Army stationed in Jiashan has sent approximately 500 to 600 wounded soldiers from the front line for treatment. Unexpectedly, at about 7:00 PM the night before last (23rd), more than 100 wounded soldiers were discharged from the hospital and caused disturbances in the roads and streets. Local police and the Zhejiang Provincial Security Team went to suppress and stop them, resulting in a conflict. The wounded soldiers gathered more and more, intending to go to the Tenth Company of the Third Battalion of the Seventh Regiment of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Team in Yangwangmiao to rob weapons. The Security Team had already been prepared and patrolled in full force, stepping up security. The merchants and residents in the city all closed their doors. The Jiashan County Government sent a telegram to Hang Yi, Commander of the Jiaxing-Huzhou Bandit Suppression, for instructions. Commander Hang immediately transferred the First Battalion and Second Company of the Second Regiment of the Security Team stationed in Jiaxing, led by Company Commander Ye Muchao, with 160 soldiers, and Xu Pucheng, District Chief of the First District of the Water Police stationed in Jiaxing, sent a patrol team led by Team Leader Wang Deqing. They all set off from Jiaxing overnight to Jiashan to suppress the disturbances. At that time, the Tenth Company of the Third Battalion of the Seventh Regiment of the Security Team in Jiashan had surrounded the wounded soldiers and escorted them back to the 34th Rear Hospital. The situation was completely resolved by 10:00 PM, and local order was restored to normal. As a result, it was reported that seven or eight wounded soldiers were injured and eleven were captured, while two security guards were injured. At that time, the No. 9 night passenger train from Hangzhou to Shanghai on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway passed through Jiaxing Station. Knowing that there was a conflict between wounded soldiers and the police and military in Jiashan, the No. 9 night passenger train was detained in Jiaxing. It did not depart from Jiaxing until 11:15 PM. More than 100 patrolmen from the Second District Patrol Team of the Water Police stationed in Jiaxing accompanied the train to Jiashan for protection. Therefore, the No. 9 night passenger train arrived at Shanghai Station at about 1:00 AM the next morning (24th).

Construction of a Telegraph Machinery Manufacturing Plant 97

The Ministry of Transportation believes that the demand for telegraph machinery and materials by various telegraph bureaus is quite large. If all are ordered from overseas, it would be uneconomical and would not meet urgent needs. Therefore, it is planning to establish a telegraph machinery factory and a battery factory to meet the demand. The telegraph machinery factory will be located at the same site as the electrical material storage and transfer office on Avenue des Soeurs in the Public Concession. The battery factory will be located in Zhoujiadu, Pudong. The products of the two factories are still applicable. However, as it has been a long time, many of the original buildings have collapsed and urgently need repair. Moreover, the telegraph machinery factory accidentally caught fire this spring, destroying the buildings. However, various lathes and machines inside the factory were only superficially burned by the fire and were not damaged. Therefore, they were temporarily moved to Macgregor Road, and the machines and lathes were slightly repaired to resume work. However, the buildings there are not suitable for use as a factory, and the original site on Avenue des Soeurs is too narrow and also unsuitable. Furthermore, the Ministry had established a second factory on Rue Mgr Favier the previous year, specializing in the production of wireless telegraphs. Because it was renting private houses, the location was both narrow and unsuitable. The Pudong battery factory has a spacious site with ample remaining land to build a factory. Therefore, it was decided to rebuild the factory buildings within the battery factory, merging the telegraph machinery factory and the second factory, along with the battery factory, into one. This would not only facilitate communication but also save some money. The telegraph machinery factory was ordered to conduct an on-site survey, make detailed plans, prepare a construction plan and drawings, and invite merchants to submit quotations for review. All repairs to the dilapidated and damaged parts of the original battery factory buildings should also be included in the estimates for compilation. The factory reported that it had been approved and that the New Construction and Engineering Factory had contracted the project. It is expected to be completed five months after the start of construction. In order to expedite the process, the Ministry has merged the three factories in advance and renamed them the Electrical Machinery Manufacturing Plant. Lu Guixiang was appointed as the factory director, and Lin Jian, the original director of the first factory, was appointed as the engineer of the first workshop. Kang Qinggui was appointed as the engineer of the second workshop, and Hu Guoguang, the original director of the battery factory, was appointed as the engineer of the third workshop. The remaining design and material staff were assigned from the original employees of each factory. Before the new factory buildings in Pudong are completed, the office will be temporarily located at the original site of the second factory at No. 27 Macgregor Road.

Yesterday's News of the Labor Strike at the Nichihua Cotton Mill 98

The Company Announced the Factory Opening Three Times

The Labor Side Resolutely Resisted Japanese Goods

The Labor Community Unanimously Offered Assistance

Since the Nichihua Cotton Mill in Pudong announced the opening of the factory for the second time, not a single worker has gone to work. Yesterday, it announced the opening of the factory again, but the labor side remained unmoved. Various labor unions in Pudong and Puxi jointly discussed assistance. Details are as follows:

Pudong Labor Community Jointly Discusses Assistance: Various labor unions in Pudong, in view of the Nichihua strike that has lasted for more than a month without resolution, deeply fear the impact. At the same time, because they share the same position, they could not bear to sit idly by. Therefore, at 2:00 PM yesterday, they convened a joint meeting to discuss assistance and countermeasures. More than 30 representatives from the British American Tobacco Factory Labor Union, Xiang Sheng Iron Factory Labor Union, Steamboat Loading and Unloading Labor Union, Hengda Cotton Mill Labor Union, Shanghai Automobile Labor Union, and Cotton Textile Industry Labor Union attended. Zhao Bi chaired the meeting, and Xia Menghuan served as the recorder. After the formalities, the representative of the Nichihua Labor Union reported on the course of the strike and the various conspiracies and sabotage by the factory in collusion with running dogs during the strike. Then, the discussion began, and the following key points were decided: 1. Issue a letter to all the workers of Japanese cotton mills in Shanghai in the name of the conference, urging them to rise up and support the strike. 2. Petition the Shanghai Citizens' Training Association to convene a general assembly of representatives from all labor unions in Shanghai to establish a support association for the Nichihua strike. 3. Regarding economic assistance, in addition to the Pudong labor unions donating as much as possible, also request donations from all labor unions in Shanghai. 4. Send a letter to the Cotton Mill Labor Union to convene a general assembly of representatives from Japanese cotton mill workers in Shanghai. When necessary, all Japanese cotton mill workers in Shanghai should take concerted action to provide assistance. 5, 6, and 7 are confidential.

The Company Announced the Opening of the Factory Three Times: The workers of Nichihua are taking an unusually resolute stance in this strike. Therefore, even the cunning factory has been unable to cope. Therefore, at the beginning of the strike, it announced the opening of the factory. Later, it falsely claimed that it was at the request of all the workers and announced the opening of the factory. As a result, not a single worker went to work. Helplessly, it announced the closure of the factory to threaten the workers. However, the workers remained unmoved. The Japanese were forced to tear down the announcements in front of the factory a few days ago and post new announcements outside, declaring the opening of the factory, intending to make a final struggle. From this, it can be seen that the Japanese side is eager to open the factory, and at the same time, its counter-strategies have been exhausted. Therefore, apart from opening the factory today and opening the factory tomorrow, there is no other way.

The Puxi Labor Community Acts in Unison: The Japanese cotton mills in Puxi, in view of the unusually resolute strike by the workers of the Nichihua Cotton Mill this time, and having heard that the losses during this strike were subsidized by the Japanese Cotton Mill Federation, the workers, in order to express their dissatisfaction with the company, will also take concerted action. It is heard that unless the issue is resolved by the time the new cotton is released on the market, they will take concerted action to awaken the Japanese.

The Labor Side is Determined to Resist Japanese Goods: In view of the cunning and maliciousness of the Japanese merchants, the Labor Union of the factory, in order to awaken them, if the labor unrest is not resolved in the shortest possible time, it will be determined to engage in a boycott of Japanese goods movement. At the same time, it warns all sectors of the country, please unanimously advocate for this.

Workers Strike at a Civilian Ship Repair Factory 99

Workers at a civilian ship repair factory in Dongjiadu, Pudong, went on strike on the 23rd of this month due to demands for higher wages. It was recently heard from an official of the Siming Coal and Stone Barge Industry Association that the association's barges are exclusively used to transport coal and fuel to major factories and ships and cannot be interrupted for a single day. Once the ship factory goes on strike, the number of barges will be insufficient. It is heard that the association intends to urgently petition the Party, government, and military agencies for a resolution.

Route Tenant de May 101

The Tragedy of an Overturned Car

Jia Zilin Seriously Injured and Died

The Other Three People are in Critical Condition

Yesterday (the 24th) morning at approximately 2:35 AM, a car suddenly crashed into a cement utility pole near Route Tenant de May and Rue Paul Beau in the French Concession, resulting in a tragedy of a destroyed car, a broken pole, one death, and three serious injuries. The details are recorded below:

Returning from a Banquet: Jia Zilin, a 40-year-old man from Pudong, currently residing at No. 24 Yuan Shang Li, next to the Tongren Fu Yuan Tang on Ningbo Road in the French Concession, used to work on ships. He has recently accumulated some savings and can be considered well-off. He is naturally charitable and has many friends. He owns a blue sedan, license number 11841, with a driver named Huang Xuelin, a 20-year-old man from Pudong. At approximately 8:00 PM the day before yesterday, Jia went to a banquet hosted by a friend with the surname of So-and-so in West Shanghai in his own car. After enjoying the banquet, he returned in the same car.

Flustered and Confused: There were four people in the car, one was the host Jia Zilin, one was Jia's nephew He Genfa, one was a relative Chen Liangcai, and one was the driver Huang Xuelin. Jia and the driver were sitting together in the front, and He and Chen were sitting together in the back. The car was traveling from west to east at full speed. Because West Shanghai is sparsely populated, the driver was driving boldly. Unexpectedly, when traveling on Route Tenant de May, there was a black-plated car in front, also traveling east. Jia's car, because of its strong speed, quickly overtook the car in front. Shortly after leaving ten yards away, near Rue Paul Beau, Jia's driver suddenly became flustered and confused. Due to momentary carelessness, he drove the car straight into a cement utility pole on the side of the road. The force of the impact was immense, and a tragedy ensued.

The Situation of the Tragedy: When the car hit the utility pole, the pole was broken and fell, completely destroying the car's engine, headlights, and thick glass. The car body and the glass on three sides were also damaged. As a result, the people in the car were unable to escape and were trapped inside, with their heads broken, flesh torn, brains splattered, hands broken, feet fractured, and blood flowing everywhere. All four were in extreme pain and unconscious. Fortunately, the black-plated car behind saw that Jia's car had caused an accident and immediately stopped. Two people in the car got out and saw the tragic situation. They immediately ordered the driver to put the injured people into the car and send them to Guangci Hospital for treatment. The two people hired another car and left.

One Dead and Three Injured: After the doctors immediately performed surgery and treatment, Jia Zilin died due to a fractured skull and splattered brains. He was already dying when he arrived at the hospital. He died about an hour later. The driver, Huang Xuelin, broke one leg and was seriously injured. The nephew, He Genfa, was blinded in one eye, and his body was also seriously injured. The relative Chen Liangcai broke his arm, and his face and chest were also injured. It is difficult to determine temporarily whether their lives are in danger. Jia's body was transported to his original home at Yuan Shang Li at approximately 8:10 AM yesterday by the hospital's white car, where the funeral was held.

Yesterday Noon on Xinxinqiao Street 102

Robbers Attempt Murder

Money Saved

Ma Alai Died Tragically

Yesterday at approximately 11:00 AM, a robbery and murder case occurred on the third floor of the Baokang Small Restaurant at No. 287 Xinxinqiao Street (i.e., Rue du Pont). The details are recorded as follows:

Taking a Break to Smoke: The Baokang Small Restaurant at No. 287 Xinxinqiao Street along the road is dedicated to serving general coolies. The house has a total of four floors and houses more than ten families. The front building on the third floor was rented to Chen Quanfu (37 years old) from Ningbo two months ago to open a Yanzike (opium den). Chen had a smoker named Ma Alai (47 years old) from Shaoxing who was in the business of buying paper ingot ashes. He currently lives at No. 179 Guoqing Road, Zhabei. Chen always takes a break to smoke at Chen's place after work, as is his custom.

Gun to the Waist: At approximately 9:00 AM yesterday morning, Ma and a group of friends first went to the Tonghe Tai Tinware Store on Pi Shao Nai Road, Xiaobeimen, to collect a payment of 350 yuan. Then, he went directly to Chen's place to smoke. He took out 85 yuan and paid it to his friends, asking them to leave first. The remaining 265 yuan were wrapped up and put in his pocket. At that time, Chen was preparing his opium pipe. Unexpectedly, two young men, one wearing a black gauze shirt and pants and the other wearing a white shirt and pants, both around 20 years old, suddenly broke in from downstairs. As soon as they saw Ma lying on the couch, the one in black took out a pistol from his sleeve and pressed it against Ma's waist.

Shot and Fell to the Ground: At that time, Ma knew he had encountered a robbery, but he just held on tight to his waistband and did not say a word. At that time, Chen got up and was about to intercede on his behalf. However, the one wearing white had already hurriedly exited the room. The robber with the gun, in desperation, pulled the trigger. With a bang, the bullet had already entered his waist. Ma fell in response. Chen, seeing the robber holding a pistol, did not dare to pursue him. He could only turn around and first protect the injured. At that time, there were only Chen's wife and a young child in the room. Chen urgently carried Ma downstairs, hired a rickshaw, and sent him to the Dazimingzhong police station. After the police chief briefly asked some questions, he transferred Ma to Renji Hospital.

Died in the Hospital: When Ma arrived at the police station, he temporarily deposited the 265 yuan along with a passbook at the police station. By approximately 3:00 PM, Ma's wife had heard the news and rushed over. She went to the hospital to meet Ma. At this time, he was still able to speak and his mind was clear. He died at 5:00 PM. The hospital notified the police station to transport the body to the Tongren Fu Yuan Tang morgue and report it to wait for today's examination. It is heard that the deceased's family is poor and only has one son.

Jin Rongling Suffers from Mental Illness

Commits Suicide by Throwing Himself into the Huangpu River After Arriving in Shanghai

Jin Rongling, 24 years old, from Meizhou, Yunnan, is currently studying in Japan. He usually lives at No. 1408 Ohara, outside Tokyo. He has a friend in Shanghai named Yang Gengguang, who lives at No. 1251 Route Lafayette in the French Concession. Recently, for some unknown reason, Jin suddenly suffered from severe mental illness. Therefore, his classmates planned to find a way to send him back to China. The day before, they lodged Jin at the Sugimoto Inn and bought a ticket for the Shanghai-bound Mikasamaruno ship to send Jin back to China to stay at his friend Yang's place for treatment. The ship was sailing in the ocean, and Jin suddenly called out to the ship's tea server, Wang Ashun, asking him to go ashore together. Wang was shocked to hear this and told him that they were still in the ocean, so where would there be land? Jin still wanted to land. Wang knew he was crazy and could not be reasoned with. Therefore, he locked him in the cabin to prevent accidents. Yesterday at approximately 12:00 noon, the ship arrived in Shanghai. Just as it was preparing to dock at the China Merchants North Wharf, Jin had already regained his freedom and suddenly jumped into the Huangpu River to commit suicide. He could not be rescued and sank without a trace. After docking was completed, the ship telegraphed the water police station to send investigator Wu Rongsheng on board to investigate the suicide. He reported back to the police station, and the police chief instructed him to notify his friend Yang Gengguang and inform the deceased's family.

Zhao Bingying Commits Suicide 104

Jumps into the Huangpu River and Dies

Two Suicide Notes with Sparse Words

Yesterday at approximately 3:00 PM, a young man wearing a white short shirt and pants hailed a rowboat owned by Ding Jixi, a man from Shandong, at the Yangjingbang Wharf, saying he wanted to cross the river to Pudong. When they reached the middle of the Huangpu River, he suddenly left a straw hat, a handkerchief, a fountain pen, a ballpoint pen, a pair of glasses, and a letter in the boat. He kept calling out (Why is it so hot today?), and while saying this, he walked to the bow of the boat. Taking advantage of the rower's unpreparedness, he suddenly jumped into the Huangpu River to commit suicide. His body sank without a trace. The rower was unable to rescue him. Therefore, he sent all the items he left behind to the water police station and stated the circumstances of the young man's suicide. The police chief examined the cover of the suicide note, which read: To Mr. Zhao Yixiao, No. 5 Wenfuli, not far from Zhongxing Road, Zhabei. Inside were letters to his parents and aunt, and a business card with the printed words Zhao Bingying, Executive Committee Member of the Shanghai Commercial Middle School Student Union. The suicide note was also signed Bingying. Therefore, it is undoubtedly known that the deceased's name is Zhao Bingying. However, the reason for the suicide is temporarily unknown. The police chief ordered investigator Wu Rongsheng to go to the address to investigate the deceased's family and verify the information. The two suicide notes are transcribed below:

To My Parents: Dear Parents, Your unfilial son is no longer in this world. I will repay your kindness in raising me as a dog or horse in the next life. After you receive this letter, please come and collect my body. Before I jumped into the river, I was preparing that money at home. Some of it was borrowed from him, and now I have returned it to them. So that money was used to repay others and for suicide. Some of it was used to buy opium to eat, but it was the same as not eating it. So I jumped into the river. The inn I rented on the 22nd was the inn next to the North Ocean Inn at the railway station. I don't know the signboard. These two letters were also written inside. I used the pseudonym Chen Ruikang, 20 years old, studying. Alas, I have probably enjoyed all the happiness in the world. Therefore, I really feel that there is no taste in this world. I have no choice but to commit suicide. I hope that after I die, you will not be sad and resentful. I will be happy in the underworld. Otherwise, will it increase my sins? I respectfully wish you good health and a good appetite. From your son Bingying, August 23rd. To My Aunt: Dear Aunt, I have jumped into the Huangpu River to commit suicide. After I die, please don't miss me. My parents in Shanghai, I am afraid that something unlucky will happen. I must ask you to serve them, the two old people. Please, please. From your nephew Bingying, August 23rd.

Verdict to Be Announced This Morning

After the marriage, she often returned to her mother's house, resulting in a very weak relationship between the couple. On the 4th of this month, Wang went out to work, and his mother-in-law, Huang Xie, suddenly took Asan away. When Wang returned home, he was told by his neighbor, Wang Ar'er, and others, so he went to his in-laws' house to pick up his wife, but was unable to. He hired a lawyer to sue Huang and others in the Shanghai District Court. The case has not yet been concluded. Recently, Huang Kunshan also filed a lawsuit in the Special District Court against his son-in-law for murdering his daughter. The other day, Wang Tingliang was summoned for questioning. Wang Tingliang explained the situation and invited Wang Ar'er and others to testify. Judge Cheng verified the testimony and said that since this case was already being litigated in the District Court, it should be submitted for judgment and there was no need for further accusations. Moreover, the allegations were unfounded, so he dismissed the plaintiff's lawsuit and declared Wang Tingliang innocent.

Robbery in the Shiliupu Area 114

Two People Shot and Seriously Injured

At 11:25 last night, three robbers suddenly came to Xu's Chicken and Duck Shop at No. 16, Xiexing Li, Shiliupu, Nanshi. Each of them was holding a handgun. They ransacked the shop, taking away clothes and cash totaling about 290 yuan. As they were leaving, the shop owner's wife, Xu Jishi (37 years old, from Jiangbei), resisted and was shot by the robbers. One bullet hit her in the neck. The shop assistant, Wang Dengfu, shouted for help and was also shot by the robbers in the chest. Both bullets pierced through. The shop assistants then took the injured people to Baolong Hospital by car and reported to the First Section of the First District Police Station. According to the doctor, Wang Dengfu's injuries were fatal and extremely dangerous. It was heard that the woman, Xu Jishi, had just given birth three days ago and was so frightened that her life was also in danger.

Robbery on Laod Road Yesterday Morning 115

One Robber Apprehended on the Spot

Around 6:10 yesterday morning, three robbers broke into No. 288, Laod Road, in the Public Concession. One of them was carrying a handgun and forbade anyone from making a noise while they ransacked the place. The total loss of gold and silver jewelry was estimated to be about 1,000 yuan. However, one of the robbers with the handgun was walking a little slower and was apprehended by two Chinese constables. The handgun and several stolen items were taken to the police station for investigation.

Thugs Forcibly Seize Animals 116

Drowning Two Monkeys

Li Song and Yang Jiu from Guangdong spent a huge sum of money to purchase twelve foreign parrots (that can speak human language) and two monkeys from abroad. They arrived in Shanghai on the Jisheng steamboat, which docked at the Qichang pier in Pudong at 2 p.m. yesterday. Li and Yang were about to hire a sampan to cross the river when suddenly more than ten vagrants came to the pier. Finding these kinds of animals to be very strange, they tried to forcibly seize them from Li and Yang, but failed. As a result, two monkeys were thrown into the river and drowned instantly. Li and others were furious and blew the police whistle, shouting that they had been robbed. Shen Yingnan, the patrolman from the Third Section of the Public Security Bureau, led the police to the scene and apprehended two vagrants, Chen Shaogen and Zhang Xiaoxiang (from Qingjiang). Together with Li, Yang, and witness Luo Riji, they were taken to the Third District. After a brief interrogation by the district chief, because Li and others were eager to board the ship for export and did not have time to get involved in litigation, Chen and Zhang were each sentenced to ten days of detention as a warning. The twelve parrots were allowed to be claimed.

Suicide Due to Difficult Living Conditions 117

Zhang Yuntian from Zhenjiang lived in the Yangjing District of Pudong and worked as a tea room attendant in the Coal Tax Bureau. He had a large family to support, but his salary was very meager. At a time when rice was as precious as pearls and firewood was as expensive as cassia, it was not enough to maintain a living, causing his wife to complain and his children to cry. He suffered a major mental blow and developed a mental illness. The other day, he had an argument with his wife over the issue of firewood and rice. Zhang then swallowed opium to commit suicide. He was sent to the hospital for treatment after being discovered, but eventually died. His body was taken home. Later, the Second Section of the Third District ordered the local police to report to the court yesterday for an autopsy. Zhang Huanping, his younger brother, then petitioned the court to waive the autopsy.

Suicide Out of Anger Over a Stolen Long Gown 118

The Old Woman Who Stole the Long Gown Deserves to Be Punished

Wang Arui, a 41-year-old stove worker from the Xinhuaizhong Hotel on Hankou Road, was from Ningbo and lived at No. 108, Mingyuan Fang, Huade Road. The other day, he happened to be off work and resting at home. He had extra rooms for rent, and there was a "room for rent" sign posted on the door. Around 10 a.m. yesterday morning, an old woman, approaching sixty, came in to inspect the rooms. Taking advantage of the opportunity, she stole Wang's short silk gown. Shortly after, she said goodbye and left. Wang discovered it afterwards, but the gown had disappeared. He cried out in despair and had an argument with his wife. Wang Arui then left in a rage and secretly committed suicide by inhaling raw tobacco. Around 12 p.m., he returned home and collapsed on the bed, moaning and vomiting repeatedly. His wife suspected that he had drunk too much and sent him to Tongren Hospital for treatment. However, the poison was irreversible, and medicine was ineffective, and he passed away. It was heard that Wang only had one daughter named Amao, who was only nine years old. The family was in dire straits, and he took his own life because of a long gown. It was so tragic.

Lawyer Wu Baodi is Accused 119

Lawyer Wu Baodi is a director of the Nanshi Charity Group and legal counsel for the Tongren Fuyuan Hall. The Hall's property includes a row of bungalows north of the District Court, with two rooms rented out by Tian Jinshan from Nantong as a sub-landlord. In 1928, Wu Baodi represented the Fuyuan Hall in suing Tian Jinshan in the District Court for owing more than 200 yuan in rent, requesting a judgment for compensation and eviction. The court ruled in favor of Wu Baodi's request, ordering Tian Jinshan to vacate the house. Tian Jinshan lost the lawsuit repeatedly, so he harbored a grudge against Wu Baodi. He once poured feces in Wu's office, which Wu reported to the police, and Tian Jinshan was arrested. Tian Jinshan was subsequently sentenced to two months of imprisonment by the court. After his release, Tian was still unwilling to give up. He went to Wu's office daily with a written grievance on his back. Later, he was detained and confined in a reformatory for more than half a year, but was eventually released again. After his release, Tian still refused to give up. He repeatedly sued Wu Baodi in court, saying that he did not owe rent and that the rent receipt had been stolen, etc. However, the court rejected his claims five or six times because they were unsupported. However, Tian still did not give up and filed a complaint with the Jiangsu Higher Court, accusing Wu Baodi of having local bully behavior and hobbies, etc. The Higher Court believed that since a lawyer was accused, the truth should be investigated, so it sent the case back to the District Court for investigation. The Prosecutor's Office dispatched Prosecutor Yang Wenjun to handle the case. The other day, a summons was issued, scheduling a preliminary hearing for the investigation court on the morning of the 27th of this month.

Preview of the Weileyuan Opening 120

The Weileyuan, which promotes bicycle racing, has been working hard and preparing meticulously for six months. The construction aspect has been completed, and other arrangements are also in place. The grand opening ceremony will be held at the end of this month, introducing this new style of Western recreation to Shanghai, providing people with an opportunity to appreciate it and feast their eyes. From now on, citizens will have one more outdoor place to spend their leisure time after work, seeking proper entertainment that can adjust their lives and benefit their physical and mental health. Therefore, since the news of the opening was announced, public interest has been very strong. According to the park's announcement, in addition to a grand program on the opening night, a grand banquet will be held the following night. The McInnes Military Band will be invited to play special music on both nights to entertain the guests. Arrangements have been finalized. In recent days, the jockeys have been stepping up their training, and hundreds of people have come from near and far to watch. Due to interference with the project, they had to implement a policy of closing the door to guests. The park is located next to Haig Road in western Shanghai. The scale and style are modeled after the Weimian Park in Paris. The track is strong, and the grandstand is comfortable, not much different from Paris. The entire venue can accommodate 9,000 spectators, and everyone can see clearly without any obstruction. Inside the track, there are boxes and hundreds of specially set elegant seats, which are closer to the track, giving a panoramic view of the competition. It is also close to the dance hall in the venue. The dance hall has a smooth floor and is located outdoors with fresh air, unlike the dirty and unhygienic indoor halls. It is a unique feature in Shanghai's dance halls. There are three bars in the venue, providing attentive service and readily available to guests. The competition is scheduled to begin at 9:30 p.m. and end at 1:00 a.m., but spectators can enter the venue as early as 8:00 p.m. for a large meal and dance. There are a total of more than one hundred jockeys from various countries. The program is easily varied and exciting. On the opening night, there will be special performances. Mr. Pengsheng, a famous coach from Sweden, will present his blood and crystallization of six months to the general public of sports enthusiasts.

Sixth District, First Precinct 121

Solved a Robbery and Assault Case

Zhang Aigen Confesses to the Robbery Without Denial

Gui Heshang from Nanxiang planted a flower garden at the residence of Dr. Bert (transliteration), a German doctor at No. 557 Sheshan Road in Western Shanghai. On the morning of the 14th of this month, he was carrying flowers and riding a bicycle from west to east. As he was passing the roadside in front of the foreign gun club on the west side of Hongqiao Road, three people suddenly blocked his way. Without asking questions, they drew their knives and committed the crime. The garden owner, Bert, rushed him to Baolong Hospital for treatment. Afterwards, Bai Zhenquan, the patrolman from the police station in charge, went to the hospital to investigate and inquired in detail about the reasons for the crime. Gui Heshang reported that there were a total of three perpetrators at the scene, one of whom was Zhang Aigen, who ran a restaurant at Wang Mansi Bridge, (also known as A Gen) (son of Zhang Qingtang, who ran a butcher shop at Zhoujia Bridge). The other two were not well known. After the crime, they robbed him of 148 yuan in cash and a bicycle and fled east. At that time, the garden owner rushed him to the hospital and did not report to the police, Bai reported after. Patrolman Bai reported after receiving the report, with the facts reported, that the case was serious. He then sent the police to the restaurant to arrest Zhang Aigen, but Zhang had already fled. The other night, Patrolman Bai learned of the whereabouts of the hiding place and brought the patrol officers Liu Wenyuan and Wang Chuntai to arrest the suspect and bring him back to the station. After Wang, the police chief, seriously interrogated him, the suspect confessed his name was Zhang Aigen, also known as A Gen, 28 years old, living in Wangjialou South Wangjiatang. On the 14th of this month, he and the fugitives Chen Adidi and Xu Qinsheng committed the robbery and assault. He directly confessed that only Hu Xiangsheng had the idea to attack and etc. Wang's police chief said that the case was a daylight robbery and that he dared to injure the victim with a knife. It was against the law and the crime was heinous. In addition to sending the suspect to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for severe punishment, the patrolman was ordered to arrest the three fugitives Chen Adidi, Xu Qinsheng, and Hu Xiangsheng who had the idea to attack. The injured Gui Heshang is still being treated at Baolong Hospital.

Military Uniform Workers 122

Request No Wage Cuts

Present Three Conditions

Since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, all military uniforms and other supplies needed by the National Army have generally been prepared in Shanghai, and the general contractor distributes them to various factories for manufacturing. Therefore, a portion of the garment industry has become specialized in the production of military uniforms. There are eight groups, namely Ningbo, Hangzhou, Yangzhou, Hubei, Shanghai (i.e., local group), Pudong, etc. There are more than fifty workers in total. However, these workers have no organization. Recently, due to wage cuts by the factory, they used the name of military uniform workers from various groups to send messages to various factories, requesting that no further cuts be made to maintain their livelihoods. The original letter stated: "We, the military uniform manufacturing workers, have been increasingly impoverished due to repeated wage cuts by the factory. For example, the wage for each set of gray military uniform trousers was originally 17.5 cents, but was later reduced to 16 cents, then to 15 cents, and then to 12 cents. Now it has been reduced to only 10 cents. The wage for each set of gray interlined trousers was reduced from 18 cents to 13.5 cents. The gray cotton interlined shell, white shirt trousers, and coat interlined shell have also been reduced to 9 cents. The wage for each pair of interlined socks has been reduced to 4.5 cents. The wage for each cartridge belt has been reduced to 4.5 cents. With such repeated reductions, and the need to apply lining, and at a time when rice is as precious as pearls and firewood is as expensive as cassia, and prices are rising, the cost of living is increasing daily. The wages of other workers in commerce and industry are increasing year by year, but the wages of us military uniform workers are decreasing and not increasing. If this continues, our livelihoods will be cut off. We have no choice but to request the following requests: (1) No further wage cuts in the future, (2) Wages must be paid on the 15th and 30th of each month, (3) Increase the wage for each large piece by 5 li and for each small piece by 2 li or more." Please indicate your accommodation within the shortest period of time. "We are grateful," etc.

South Shanghai Tobacco Exchange Industry The South Shanghai Tobacco Exchange Industry vigorously promotes domestic product publicity. Currently, foreign merchants sell Gu Yin brand cigarettes in boxes of ten, through salesmen with trays, to the front of various industry shops, hindering the livelihoods of colleagues. The boxes are printed with the words "Made in China," which is obviously imitating the name of Chinese merchants and harming the Chinese people's psychology of promoting domestic products. The association has previously sent a letter to the association, requesting the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to investigate and prohibit it in order to safeguard the rights of Chinese merchants. The association has submitted a report to the superior authorities for processing. It is heard that the company has received this news and has withdrawn the trays. A part of Nanshi held another meeting yesterday to report on the progress of the work. The following proposals were made: (1) The tax bureau's treatment of colleagues in the Chinese Concession is unfair. The formalities for Chinese tobacco must be checked and stamped, which is cumbersome and costly. As for foreign merchants selling tobacco, they feel that it is convenient. Resolved: Request the association to submit a request to the government for a ruling in order to unify and avoid suffering. (2) The investigators asked colleagues to investigate their names, the amount of capital, and the total number of cigarette sales. The registration has already been registered, but the Social Bureau has not yet registered the industry registration. What is their intention? Resolved: Send a letter to the association to inquire about the details. (Finally) The promotion of domestic products should continue to be vigorously promoted, and other important cases were discussed and dispersed.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather along the national coast and the Yangtze River basin is sunny and hot. Seasonal winds are from the southwest to southeast. The weather south of Ogasawara is bad due to a hurricane moving north. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 96.6 and the lowest was 77.7.

Letter

Dear Editor,

I am writing to inform you that the report on the collision between the Jiangjing and Daji ships as published in your newspaper these past few days does not match the facts. According to what happened, the two ships were sailing from the lower reaches to Shanghai at 5:25 AM on the 21st. The Daji was in front and the Jiangjing was behind, passing the first buoy in Dashatou. The Daji was moving towards the buoy, so it took a slight turn, and had already reached the second buoy. The Jiangjing did not turn, but continued straight ahead. The Daji sounded two signals as a warning, but the Jiangjing still continued straight, and suddenly crashed into the Daji's stern from the left, causing great damage to the second and third decks and the lower iron plate of the Daji. The bow of the Jiangjing was also slightly damaged. The Shanghai Customs Officer and the Hesperus are currently inspecting the loss to both ships. We will determine the measures to be taken after investigating the faults of both parties, and therefore, we especially send this letter to correct the record. I hope you will publish it in the letter section. Best regards, Shanghai Dada Steamboat Company, August 24.

China Expedition

Soccer Team Ties Surabaya China

One to One... Eleventh Battle Report

(Surabaya, August 6) After two victories by the China Expedition Soccer Team in Surabaya, their reputation has been revived. Therefore, in the third match (Wednesday) against the China Club, everyone expected the China Expedition Team to win. Those who used the soccer match for gambling all gave China one to two goals. Unexpectedly, it ended in a tie, which is a pity. The fact is that the strength of the Chinese Expedition Team and the Chinese Second Team, whether in attack or defense, was superior. In terms of soccer skills, the Chinese Team was far behind. The Chinese Team was only diligent and commendable, and they gave their all in rushing and defending, which resulted in a tie. In addition, the China Expedition Team's front line was unwilling to be too pressing, seemingly to save some face for the Chinese Team. Whenever the Chinese goal was in danger, Dai, the center forward, and the left winger would not rush to attack, but just stand by and watch. If they had been as brave as when they played against the national team, the number of times they would have been broken through would have been countless. From the surface of this 70-minute battle, there were mutual attacks and defenses, and the strength was comparable, but in terms of actual skills, the Chinese Team was far inferior to the China Expedition Team. It was lucky that they could tie.

(1) Reduced Spectators on Non-Holidays

Today is not a holiday, and spectators from various ports are unable to come from afar. Many local spectators are also tied up by official duties, so they cannot attend as scheduled, so it is almost half empty. It is said that the income is also 5,000 to 6,000 shields.

The China Expedition Team was stronger, and the Chinese Team was still trapped. Just when the defense was urgent, the referee blew the whistle to rest. In the first half, China took the lead with a score of one to zero.

(6) Chen Jiaqiu Replaces Fu Xiangqing

In the second half, the battle continued. At 5:20, right forward Fu Xiangqing was injured in the leg and could not continue to play. Chen Jiaqiu was replaced. After the contact, the battle became more intense. The China Expedition Team tried to retaliate, while the Chinese Team wanted to maintain its victory. The battle was very interesting to watch.

In order to preserve its victory, the Chinese Team attacked and defended to the death.

Chen Fuyi's defense was incompetent, and it went into the net. (9) No Gains or Losses in the Continued War

Continuing the battle, the China Expedition Team was plagued by the lucky star. Although the strength was strong, the goal was difficult to achieve. Therefore, when the referee blew the whistle to end the game, the score was still a one-to-one tie. Rotary Cup Semi-Final Third Act 129

Chinese Doubles Fail

Lost to Portugal 2-3 Yesterday

Today's Singles Match with Portugal Decides Finals Spot

British Singles Win Secures Finals Spot Against America

Yesterday marked the third act of the Shanghai Rotary Cup Tennis Tournament, featuring the doubles team from China against Portugal and the singles teams from Britain and America. Britain's Wheatley defeated America's Squire 3-1. Over the past three days, Britain has won two singles matches and one doubles match, losing only one singles match. Having secured a 3-1 victory, Britain has earned the right to compete in the finals and will not play today, preparing instead for the final showdown. The Chinese doubles team fell short of victory, ultimately losing to the Portuguese team 2-3. Consequently, the fate of China and Portugal in their fight for a finals spot will depend on the outcome of today's matches.

(1) Britain Secures Finals Spot 6|4

6|4

(British) Wheatley ○|6 Squire

6|○

The strength of Britain and America is almost equal. Britain, relying on the efforts of veteran Wheatley, who participates in both singles and doubles matches, has succeeded in all three events, achieving a 3-1 victory over Britain and securing a spot in the finals. In recognition of their contributions, veteran Wheatley deserves the top spot.

At the beginning of the match, both sides showed their skills and held their ground. Each player held an advantage when serving, and the number of games progressed evenly. Neither side yielded, resulting in a 4-4 tie. Then, Squire was the first to break the deadlock, ultimately failing with a self-inflicted error. With the balance broken, Wheatley added another game, winning the first set 6-4.

In the second set, Wheatley's momentum continued, achieving favorable results in every match. Their amazing skills were evident in their self-inflicted errors and victories against the enemy. Soon, they held a commanding lead of 5-1. Squire, young and strong, fought back hard, unexpectedly winning three consecutive games, narrowing the difference to 4-5. Wheatley, mature and steady, continued to demonstrate their skills and successfully completed the set, winning again 6-4.

In the third set, Squire's spirit was strong, moving swiftly as if a brilliant first set was occurring. The veteran Wheatley, enjoying the spoils of victory, lacked energy, making the outcome even easier to achieve. One of the most distinctive features was their sudden advance to the net during the back-and-forth rallies, succeeding in every situation, both left and right, thus winning the set 6-0. During this match, the audience, including the British, were fascinated and amazed.

After three sets, a brief rest was taken. Not long after, the players returned to the court and the intense battle resumed. Considering Wheatley's defeat in the third set due to age and fatigue, most observers believed Squire had a chance in the fourth set. However, Wheatley's physical strength had already recovered. Their forehand and backhand returns were varied, and Squire struggled to move forward amidst the difficulties, losing game after game until they suffered a complete defeat of 0-6. As a result, Britain's Wheatley won 3-1.

Important News

Ministry of Education 135

Issues Circular on Continuing to Handle New Budgets According to Old Regulations

The Ministry of Education, upon the order of the Executive Yuan, announced that the budget preparation for the 18th year would continue to be implemented according to the budget regulations of the 17th year. The circular was sent to national universities and the education departments of various provinces and cities. The Executive Yuan's 2970th order stated, "Regarding the matter, the Executive Yuan presented, 'Regarding the transfer of the matter, the Ministry of Finance presented, 'The 18th year has now ended. It is proposed that the preparation of all final accounts continue to be implemented in accordance with the budget regulations of the 17th year in order to facilitate convenience. We humbly request that you transfer it to the government for review.' Upon investigation, the case of preparing the final accounts for the 17th year had previously been drafted by this department in accordance with the regulations and formats, and submitted to your esteemed court for transfer to the National Government for promulgation. Subsequently, due to the failure of various agencies inside and outside the capital to submit them on time, this department again received approval to extend the deadline by three months and separately issued reminders. To date, the extended deadline has been exceeded, and the submissions from various agencies are still incomplete. Moreover, the end of the 18th year is approaching, and the methods for preparing the final accounts urgently need to be determined so that various agencies can prepare them in a timely manner and complete them as soon as possible. Furthermore, since the budget regulations for the 17th year are feasible, it is proposed that the preparation of the final accounts for the 18th year be continued in accordance with the same format to avoid unnecessary changes. The Audit Yuan was contacted to solicit opinions, and a reply was received stating that the old regulations are still feasible. However, each agency should create an extra copy of the final account report when preparing it and send it to the Audit Yuan for preliminary review in order to avoid delays. Please handle accordingly.' Based on this, we have prepared a document and submitted it to your esteemed court for transfer to the National Government for review. If approved, we also request that you issue a circular instructing that the years stipulated in the old budget regulations for the 17th year be advanced by one year, and that no further regulations be issued to avoid complexity." Based on this, upon investigation, the budget regulations for the 17th year were previously issued by this government's 833rd order. Based on the aforementioned situation, apart from issuing an order stating, "The presentation has been noted. The request should be approved and a circular issued for compliance. This order should be disseminated for knowledge," a joint order is issued instructing compliance and also instructing subordinates to comply accordingly. This order." Based on this, apart from issuing separate orders, a joint order is issued instructing the department to immediately comply and also instruct subordinates to comply accordingly. This order." Based on this, apart from issuing separate orders, a joint order is issued instructing compliance. This order."
